                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Reflecting on the Past and Striving Harder
<Prayer> Today is October 4, 1967, which corresponds to the first day of the ninth month in the lunar calendar. How much blood and tears have you shed to choose this insignificant nation among many and to establish it in the vast land of three thousand ri? 
Though our outward appearance may be insignificant, I hope we can maintain a loyal heart before the Father and a posture that can long for the Father. 
I hope that the Father's grief will be resolved and that the second liberation will be realized on this land. May the sad day of October 4, twelve years ago, not end in sorrow but become a day to give honor and glory to the Father. 
I hope to become children who can represent the Father. 
Please allow your blessed and precious children to fulfill their priestly mission. 
I earnestly hope that the will may be fulfilled centering on these seven countries: Korea, Japan, the United States, the United Kingdom, Germany, France, and Italy. I offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 
October 4, 1967 (Wed) 8 AM, Former Headquarters Church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* These words were spoken during the commemorative worship service for the release from Seodaemun Prison, compiled from notes taken by former President Yoo Woo-hwan and recorded by the Historical Compilation Committee Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol, as well as from <Seonghwa> No. 70 (October 1967). The title was added by the editor. 
8   Reflecting on the Past and Striving Harder
<Summary of the Words> Today is October 4 in the solar calendar, which corresponds to the first day of the ninth month in the lunar calendar. 
The Teacher has had no joyful days in the past 21 years. This year marks the end of the Teacher's 21-year course and your 7-year course. There are three months left in the solar calendar and four months left in the lunar calendar this year. 
Our blessed families, dedicated to the will, must live with the same destiny. 
The 36 families stand in the position of ancestors, while the other families must establish a family that has never existed in history as children. 
We must examine whether our current position, centered on God and the Parents, is not embarrassing in front of the children growing up and the world to come. 
When faced with any difficult or awkward situation, we should not resolve it as we please. If we quietly think about how God would resolve such matters, the solution will naturally come to mind. At that time, we must engage in decisive action. 
We have developed to this extent because we have struggled with the insufficient devotion we have built until now. However, we must recognize that it was God's efforts behind the scenes that allowed us to reach this standard. This can be understood even from the Teacher's 21-year course. We must know how much God has worked behind the scenes to bring us to this point. 
To establish the Korean nation, countless ancestors' blood has been connected to find this day. When we see this, we feel how inadequate we are. 
It is true that we have all resolved to go out for the will. We have sworn to restore the nation and the world. And we are acting according to that resolution. Therefore, God has the responsibility to lead us. 
Until now, we have walked this path centered on the nation. However, we must now advance beyond the world to the cosmos as individuals and families. If we cannot achieve it in our time, we must leave a will for our descendants to fulfill the purpose. Even if we die early, we must be grateful to God for guiding us while we were alive and thank Him for the will. We must leave with a sense of regret toward the Teacher for not being able to fulfill the will completely. 
We cannot let our guard down for even a moment. We must always be in a state of readiness for battle. We must carry a weapon and shield. When the 7-year course ends, the responsibilities of this nation will come to us. Now is the time to assign you greater responsibilities and missions. Each of you must resolve to reflect on the past and make new commitments for the future. 
When we think of the facts known only to God and the Teacher, we feel that there are things that need to be settled again. 
We must compare how different the 'me' at the start of the will is from the 'me' today, reflect on it, and resolve to be more loyal than at the beginning. We must become a self that surpasses the self at the start in every aspect. We must also have a more earnest heart than at the beginning. 
The Teacher is also in a serious position, reflecting and needing to settle things while comparing the time when the will began and today, as the 21-year course is coming to an end. 
We must be more earnest emotionally than at the beginning and more active than at the beginning. 
Now we must walk the second 7-year course. The 36 families, 72 families, 124 families, among these, the 7-year course of the 36 families is more important than that of individuals. 
We must reflect on whether the 7-year course we have walked has been centered on heart. We must become a foundation that God can remember and that the environment of the past can testify to. If we have not done so until now, we must make a new determination to become such a foundation from now on. 
The question today is how my own self can bear historical fruit. Individuals must be connected vertically to the Teacher and horizontally with their family members, understanding that they are going together. Even if we cannot share the same heart, life, and actions with the Teacher, we must at least share the same direction and heart. 
Until now, those called on earth have fought on earth. The fight on earth is for the purpose of indemnifying everything, so the joy and victory during this period are not theirs. They must become a sacrifice for greater joy and victory. Therefore, after victory, they must aim for something greater. 
Only we, the Unification Church members, know God's will, so we must open the path that has been blocked for us. Until now, we have fought centered on the nation in suffering. 
10   Reflecting on the Past and Striving Harder
We must have an attitude of trying to understand the tears in the Teacher's life. And we must always have the heart to walk the same path as the Parents. 
The grief of history that has come down must be resolved centered on this nation. This grief must be resolved through me and my family, and the emotional standard must be clear that it must be resolved through the process of reconciliation. 
For us, the heavy responsibility is how much we can gather the sad history of the past and establish a joyful historical path in our time. 
The restoration of the individual and the family also has external and internal stages. 
We must become a self that does not leave behind the words, "It would have been better if you had not been born." 
Even now, I often think of many things that make my teeth grind. The betrayal of those who swore to share the Teacher's will, the extension of the indemnity restoration course to 21 years, and so on. These are still issues I think about. 
The sins they have committed are tribal, not national or global. Therefore, it cannot exceed the next 21 years. We must restore them as well. Forgiving from the position of having to repay the enemy is God's love. God loved fallen humanity more than He loved unfallen humanity. 
After the 7-year course, the efforts will remain as the results of victory. The 36 families stand in the position of ancestors up to Jacob. If the ancestors cannot take responsibility, the descendants must. 
Now that the 7-year course is ending, we must reorganize the blessed families. 
Those who cannot be salvaged must be replaced. 
When blessed, their position and connections change, but there is no change in the essence itself. Blessed families stand in the position of representing the whole. Blessing is a promise for the future world. Blessed families must become families where God is present and stand in a position to share blessings with all people. 
Blessed families must become a source that descendants can revere. They must leave behind the heart of the Father and the memory of those who longed for the Father. 
11 
In the remaining three months, we must reflect on the past 7 years and consider whether God is pleased with me or not. * 
2)
Losers and Winners
<Summary of the Words> The birthplace of the Principle Study Association is Korea. However, today, the Principle Study Association in Japan has gained worldwide attention through the media. 
Initially, there were many difficulties, including opposition demonstrations by some parents, but today a global foundation has been laid. Now, even the Japanese National Assembly and police support this Principle movement. No matter how problematic it may be, victory is ours. This is because we have an ideology that must win. 
49 media outlets have been mobilized to report on the Principle Study Association. The organ of the Japanese Communist Party, <Akahata>, includes the Principle Study Association among its three major targets for overthrow, and I have heard that it has also been published in the People's Daily of China and the Soviet Communist Party's organ. 
However, when we consider whether the Principle Study Association in Korea, the birthplace of this movement, has the ability to push the wave of the Principle movement forward globally, the answer is no. 
So what should we do? 
There is a saying that it is better to have a disabled child in the family than to have none at all. In the past, the Teacher needed 3,000 to 7,000 university graduates to fight for the restoration of South Korea (the Principle movement), but that did not happen. So, high school graduates were brought in. 
Historically, most of the figures who have accomplished great things were not necessarily PhDs; they were individuals with determination unrelated to them. Those who seemed reckless to others became historical figures. In other words, history has been woven by those who are fighters. 
The Teacher does not yield to any past saints or to anyone in the present or future in enforcing his beliefs. 
When considering the achievements of young people who fought on the front lines for 4 or 5 years after finishing high school and the achievements of all of you, you cannot match them. The question is how to take care of the past and cultivate new sprouts. 
The title of today's message is "Losers and Winners." Can we say that anyone with a good sign and good character is a winner? Conversely, can we say that anyone with a bad sign and bad character is a loser? No, that is not the case. The question depends on how strong, resilient, and solid one is. 
So, is there anyone who is strong, resilient, and solid? This is the factor that determines victory and defeat. 
To become a winner, first, one must have an ideology. In other words, to be strong, one must have self-confidence. God also loves the prayers of brave people overflowing with confidence, even in the most lonely and risky positions. The victory of a person without confidence is a false victory. 
Second, one must make a decisive decision. Pour 120 percent of your energy into it! If you still lose after that, it is not a loss. A co-worker will surely appear. 
Those who sleep when others sleep, eat when others eat, and play when others play will lose. There is bound to be hunger on the path of struggle. The Teacher had no day without hunger until the age of 30. 
The time for the Teacher's struggle has not yet come. 
We must cultivate the conviction to gracefully overcome pain, sadness, loneliness, frustration, and injustice with joy. How can one make a decisive decision without a resolution? 
To become a winner, one needs ideology, self-confidence, a decisive decision, and, thirdly, struggle. 
14   Losers and Winners
When you have an ideology, make a decisive decision, and struggle, victory will surely follow. * 
3)
Pour Everything into the Final Battle
<Summary of the Words> Today, as you know, is the Day of Children corresponding to the last year of the 7-year course. And this year is the last year of the 21-year course for the Teacher. 
Among the four major holidays, only God's Day remains undecided. There must also be a Day of the Family. A family that has been restored must have a Day of the Family. The family of the Teacher, who has fulfilled the expectation of a son-in-law, and at least the 36 families need this first. However, when considering how many families are truly taking the lead in this restoration process, we have no face before God. 
From now on, you must make a new determination and fight nationally during the second 7-year course. The first 7-year course has been led centered on the Teacher. However, the second 7-year course must be advanced centered on the 36 families. 
Now that this 7-year course is ending, our families must also be reorganized. Every family must have a Day of the Family, and families that do not have this position must prepare to have it within the next two months. If there are words that have not been said between couples, they should gather the children together and publicly discuss them to make new commitments for the future. 
November 2, 1967 (Thu), Former Headquarters Church.
* These words were spoken on the 8th Day of Children and compiled from <Seonghwa> No. 71 (November 1967) and notes recorded by the Historical Compilation Committee Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol. 
16   Pour Everything into the Final Battle
Why do we need the Day of Children, the Day of Parents, the Day of All Things, and God's Day? These days exist for the completion of the purpose of creation. You must express gratitude to the spiritual world and to the pioneering members on this day. You must understand how important this Day of Children is centered on God. 
If the human ancestors had not fallen, this day would have been established on the foundation of Adam and Eve's victory, and it would have been a day to share joy together. Therefore, today we would have celebrated the restored Day of Children. 
You must do everything in good times or sad times, and also when boasting, centered on the Father. Likewise, from the Father's position, He must also handle all these situations centered on the children. This is the relationship between parents and children. 
Joy and sorrow are represented by the names of heaven and hell. When the Teacher first embarked on this path, he pondered what the fundamental essence of the universe is. It is the relationship between the Father and the Son. Therefore, the fundamental content of restoration is the connection between father and child. History must restore this relationship. Thus, the history of restoration is to restore the original relationship between the Father and the sons and daughters.
Regardless of whether it is a joyful or sad event, it must be reported before the Father. The path of restoration lies in how to create more joyful circumstances before the Father, and it is also the path of filial piety. 

We must report to God at all times, whether we are awake or asleep, and become victorious beings. After that, we must be connected emotionally and become sons centered on the Father, while parents must do so through their children. As we come forth centered on the Father, we must ensure that He can find comfort through us, and we must connect so that all of humanity can unite through this bond via our nation.

The Teacher's prayers are not many, nor are they numerous. They are centered solely on restoring the relationship of true parents centered on God, families centered on true parents, children centered on families, and tribes centered on children. 

After restoring Korea, England must be restored, but Japan is currently taking its place. 

First, Korea, Japan, the United States, and Germany must be restored. As the Unification Church is a matter of concern in Korea, the Principle Study Group is a matter of concern in Japan. It must be a matter of concern because the Japanese graduate Principle Study Group corresponds to the position of the children of the Unification Church.

After restoring these four countries—Korea, Japan, the United States, and Germany—England, France, and Italy must be restored. Together, these countries make seven.

Before seeking the tribe, the family must fulfill its responsibilities, and before seeking the nation, one must reflect on whether they have fulfilled their responsibilities before the tribe. In the final battle, one must pour out everything they have. What remains is only life. We must be in a position to offer even this life. One must pour out all they have until God tells them to stop.

Restoration begins with tears. Do not be ashamed to move forward toward the glorious position, and become someone who can accept 100% of any advice given.

You do not realize how significant your mission is and how important your position is. Therefore, you are in a fearful position. Among the 36 families, at least one family must live with their parents.

Husbands and wives must kneel facing each other and pray. 

The Teacher's life is conducted from an absolute position. There is not even a vague notion. 

To embark on the path of the will, one must have a different resolve from the start. It is important to know in advance that it is not a path that anyone can take. A resolution is good, but if that resolution ends in failure, it will bind me. To avoid failure, some external force must support me. In other words, God must be the motivation.

It is not a matter of how many years I have been on this path. The question is whether I have helped on this path during that time or incurred a debt. Even a very short moment is serious for the Teacher. Who can guarantee that they will not die at any moment? A very brief instant can be the turning point where I gain life or lose it, so how serious is that? Air and food are absolute conditions for our lives.

We often swear and resolve. However, because we waver repeatedly, we are told not to swear. There should be no oaths on the path of love.

Can the couples of the world love each other, or can parents love their children, or can the martyrs love their country, without loving God as much? To become the true sons and daughters of God, one must first be praised before God, the spirit world, and descendants.

The three must align. The three points must combine to create an area. Two points alone do not suffice, as they only form a line.

When you tie your belt, tie it tightly. Those who try to work vaguely with a "let's try" attitude can never do God's work. How much have my heart and body longed for God's work?

Can the Principle, the Unification Church, and you each be separate? If these three are brothers, then the Principle and the Unification Church are the older brothers, and you are the beloved younger sibling.

Listening to the words is good, but you must also know how to jump according to the command. To restore, one must not look back at others. Restoration is something I must take responsibility for.

You must become a son who can work without any hindrance even if the Father is not present. And to be called a true son or daughter, you must have a heart greater than that of the Father, caring for your siblings and taking responsibility for all family affairs.

How joyful must God have been when He created Adam and Eve in the beginning? How much must He have loved them? The degree to which God loves Adam and Eve cannot be compared to how humans love their children. You must receive love greater than that of Adam and Eve. Otherwise, you cannot become God's legitimate children. Without receiving God's love, you cannot enter heaven. Until now, there was no realm of hope to enter and enjoy after Adam and Eve's perfection, that is, the storehouse of love. The one who comes to prepare that is the Lord of the Second Advent.

The Teacher has prayed so hard that his cotton pants and jacket have been soaked, and he has sworn while stabbing his belly with a knife countless times, and he has resolutely determined his heart millions of times while overcoming the brink of death. 

He has seen many death row inmates in prison. If they have any hope, it is only to live. If Christianity were to give them three days to repent during that time, they could be resurrected, how serious would that be? If there is a way for death row inmates to live, they would do anything. If only they are allowed to live, they would carry a cup filled with water on their forehead and walk around Seoul. It is a matter of life or death; what could they not do?

How serious was Jacob when he wrestled with the angel at the Jabbok River? If the angel fought with the heart of a representative, Jacob fought with the heart of a millennium. That is why Jacob was able to win. The loser focuses more on external things, while the winner focuses more on internal matters. The one with a higher internal standard wins.

Today's Unification Church is different in story and content from the world. The Unification Church is born from the history of suffering.

The Teacher's love for the Republic of Korea is different from that of others. The Teacher's love for humanity is also different from that of others. Likewise, the Teacher's love for God is different from your love for God. The strings are different. They must be strong and resilient. They must also have confidence. To have confidence, one must have ideology and go through the history of the past, present, and future.

The seven-year course is coming to an end. Now is the time when the Teacher can no longer step forward personally. So, he tried to put the members forward, but it did not go well. Would it be good if the Teacher led worship again? When facing you, there is not a single person who wants to open their heart and share their story.

It may seem easy to watch marathon runner Abebe run, but he has many hardships and struggles that others do not know about.

Some of you may think that since you are not even 40 yet, you are far from dying or have no connection with the grave. However, who knows if you might die while walking around today? It is a serious matter. 

Even if you are hit with a birch stick, you would be happy if it meant being sent to heaven. If you can go to heaven like that, you would boast about that place.

Become a true person. A true person has everything, so they have no desires. A true person is fulfilled to the extent that they have no desires.

The Teacher believes he has occupied the term "unification." Wearing the nameplate of unification, he endures the most criticism in the world yet stands firm without falling.

Among the true, there is only one genuine truth. If you do not resemble the true, everything else is false; therefore, all of humanity must follow and emulate the true. To become a true person, one cannot be alone. To become a true man, there must be participants. This is the principle of heaven, which is why there is a feast of the lamb. This is an event where the true man and participants appear and unite through God's true love.

One cannot exist alone. To exist, there must be relative conditions. Joy and sorrow cannot exist alone. Even God, feeling lonely, created heaven and earth. That absolute position necessitated the creation of heaven and earth.

When you say "Hey!" there must be a response of "Yes." Because Jesus could not establish a relative connection, there is not a single righteous person in heaven and earth. Thus, we cannot help but await the day of the Second Advent.

To disappear from this earth is suffering and pain. To think it would be better not to have a husband is contrary to relative principles and violates universal law. Therefore, when a husband dies, one says, "I die too." That is suffering. The more one meets all relative conditions, the happier they are. No matter how earnest, if it is simple, it is not enjoyable.

The purpose of creation must be fulfilled by completing the expectation of the son-in-law. The first is the perfection of individuality, and the second is the perfection of the expectation of the partner. The struggle between body and mind has expanded into a world war.

Humans have both the static field (love-family) and the mission field (work). When one cannot possess both, they are like the dead in the world of existence.

Jesus could not stand before God with dignity because he did not have the historical fruit of children, which is the three-object purpose between God, Adam, and Eve.

The Principle must be applied to individuals, families, societies, and nations. All existence operates on the principle of give and take. Therefore, from the organization of the human body to the earth, sun, and universe, everything engages in give and take and moves in circular motion according to that principle.

What is good? It is to serve a greater purpose. If sacrificing the entire Unification Church serves this nation and country, that is good. If sacrificing the nation and country serves the world, that is good. When the world does well, that nation becomes the central nation and the central country.

Everyone is bound to do good. From the beginning, it is said that one is bound to do good. One must do it. If they do not, they must be made to do it, even if it means being hit.

The Unification Church in Japan must work just like the Unification Church in Korea. Even if they have to sleep on the streets and beg, they must work for Japan. Only then will Japan survive.

The Unification Church must shout that it will save the world. Therefore, it must humble itself. Then the Unification Church will rise, and those who opposed it will instead become humble.

Work done on the foundation of the son-in-law expectation will not fail. If you do not create it, the Teacher will. We must fight for the will even on Sundays and carry the mission of pioneers. If a true person is encountered while walking the path, one must shed tears and be grateful.

For the sake of the country, individuals must be sacrificed. Otherwise, one becomes more of a traitor than Lee Wan-yong, who sold the country to Japan.

The Teacher does not seek to make you work hard to live well. He wants to ensure that the footsteps of descendants do not cease at your grave. To do that, you must become a true person.

It is joyful to evangelize. Conversely, if one does not evangelize, joy does not come. The Teacher also does this because it is painful not to do so. Even after being scolded for evangelizing, it brings joy.

The true cannot exist apart from God. A true person is one who establishes the three-object purpose and lives. 

**Conditions of Blessing**

Since the day the human ancestors Adam and Eve fell, humanity has been looking forward to the day when God will bless them.

Religion plays an intermediary role for that day of blessing. The Unification Church seeks to find and establish the legitimate children to inherit everything.

One cannot be blessed without going through the process of restoration. The reason is Satan. According to the standard of the will of the blessed families on earth, everything concerning the ancestors in the spirit world is determined relatively. Therefore, you have come out with the chills of your ancestors.

The Teacher has been earnest and has struggled for this day.

Blessing is inheriting the connection of true parents. Therefore, parents bless while hanging the sign of fighting against the world of Satan.

Men must become representatives of the Father, and women must become representatives of the Mother.

The reason Jesus left behind the sorrow of the bride and groom was ultimately because of the providence of blessing.

The cooperator going to the ideal world is the ideal partner.

Restoration through indemnity spans the three ages of Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent; therefore, the blessed person must establish the historical conditions of indemnity spanning three generations.

Thus, a sum of 30,000 won corresponding to the three must be needed. This is for the restoration of material.

The instruction to evangelize 12 people is given because it is necessary to indemnify the fact that Jesus' 12 disciples could not become one.

**Victory and Defeat are Decided in an Instant**

In comparison to the long history, seven years is an extremely short period. However, this seven years can also be seen as a period that determines the entire history, which is why it can indemnify 6,000 years of history.

Let us have serious moments.

No matter how great a nation may be, its downfall is decided in an instant. While having a long history is important, it is even more important to spend moments wisely.

Do not forget that the fate of history is determined in a moment of sleeping and eating. A single mistake in one day or one moment can nullify all the achievements accumulated over a lifetime. The victory or defeat of an entire life is decided in an instant. 

In a successful position, everyone praises, but when failure occurs, the opposite happens.

It may seem like our breathing will continue endlessly, but if we cannot inhale the breath we exhaled, we die. The last moment of breath determines life.

Just as a building cannot be erected without a critical decision in an instant, the completion of restoration is also determined in a moment. The process may be long, but the time of completion is instantaneous.

When looking at a mountain, one thinks of its watershed. A single rock at the summit can be the watershed. Even drops of water that fall equally flow in entirely different directions depending on their falling direction. The mission of the Teacher is to ensure that they fall in the right direction. Without even a small force applied by the Teacher, restoration cannot occur.

Unification Church members are in a position sitting at the watershed of the mountains. If one makes a mistake in this moment, it will lead to the downfall of descendants for thousands of generations.

We must tightly bind our arms and legs to God's rope, but we are in a position where we only hook our fingers and ask, "Please pull me up." God will eventually pull the rope up. But how dangerous is that state! The strength with which I hold the rope must be greater than the strength with which God pulls it up. If we hold on tightly enough, God will pull us up in an instant.

Why does God lower so many ropes? Because throughout history, no one has held that rope tightly, He always repeats that work.

There are also rotten ropes lowered by Satan. Yet people cling to them and roll around happily.

Imagine that you are taking a picture with your heart printed on the film, and you see that picture yourself. 

When it comes to holding onto God's rope, you look elsewhere with your eyes and only hold it with your hands. And you are not holding it tightly; rather, you think of it as a spectacle and hold it carelessly.

God's providence of restoration cannot be done carelessly. It is a serious matter that requires risking one's life.

Since the human ancestors fell in the beginning, their descendants also have elements of falling.
is not the way to achieve success. We must have a foundation to support our ambitions and ideals. 

We have worked hard for the sake of others, but now is the time to focus on ourselves. We have sown seeds for the nation, but we have not yet reaped the harvest. Now we are entering a stage where we can begin to reap. 

The established churches that have vehemently opposed us are now beginning to give up. They recognize that our movements are significant and that we are not merely a group that suffers losses. 

People are rational beings; they will not engage in actions that lead to their own detriment. They will only act when they see a benefit. 

In the past, many viewed the Unification Church as a losing organization, but now they see that there are benefits to be gained. 

We have conducted anti-communist lectures that reached 1.5 million people, most of whom are influential members of society. This creates a substantial foundation that can have a significant impact on our society. 

The public security bureau has noticed an increase in civilian reports of espionage since 1965. They are puzzled by the high percentage of arrests that result from civilian cooperation, unaware that we are behind this change. 

We have built a reputation and recognition from the local to the national level through our activities. 

However, we must remember that great achievements cannot be rushed. Sudden success can lead to sudden failure. We must have a solid foundation to support our ambitions and ideals. 

We must strive for greatness with a clear vision and purpose, ensuring that we do not seek immediate success without the necessary groundwork.
I want to accomplish everything in a single day, but that cannot be the case. Among you, there may be those who see opposing people and think, "Oh my! Those enemies, if only we could improve the environment with just us, without those who are not on God's side... Is God not present?" There may be some who think this way, but that is not the case. For the land to be firm, it must rain. But what if it keeps raining continuously? Nothing can be accomplished with just rain. The sun must shine as well. However, it cannot be only sunny either. There must be wind, it must be cold at times, hot at others, and it must go through cycles of freezing and thawing over a long period. The longer it goes on, the more firmly the land is compacted to obtain the true seed. To dig up that well-compacted land, one must apply greater force than what is already there. Isn't that right? 

The same applies to God's restoration providence. Would God build a headquarters to manage the world on a flimsy foundation that could easily roll away with a gust of wind? No, that is not the case. Even beggars are mobilized for this. Even the legs of the dead are mobilized to firmly establish and build the foundation. 

It would be better if the teacher could do this work quickly. It would be nice if it could be done swiftly, but why is it that I have to suffer so much, bending my back and turning my hair white? That is something no one desires. However, when it comes to doing great things, one must never rush. 

When the teacher first set out on this path, he was in his youth, just like you. As a young man in his twenties, his wish was to see the age of forty. You all know through the principles how important it is to surpass the age of forty in the restoration course. One must not die before crossing the forty threshold. One must not be exhausted or retreat. No matter how much one is pushed or chased, one must advance to the end. 

Even if there is no substantial progress over forty years, the heart must develop. The heart must strengthen its strong resolve and inner determination to cross the forty threshold. The more one is persecuted, the more it must be managed as a source of conviction to surpass the forty threshold. Those who cannot do this will fail before crossing the forty threshold. After crossing the forty threshold, a new seven-year course and a twenty-one-year course emerge. Therefore, the teacher is also going through the twenty-one-year course. 

In that process, he has experienced many hardships. He has faced much criticism. There have been all sorts of incidents and circumstances. However, these were absolutely necessary for the Unification Church to establish itself as the Unification Church. Therefore, this will become a global model course in the future. The teacher's thought is to establish a tradition through such environments and conditions. 

The period of trials until now has been a time to firmly establish roots. 

As I have come out of the seven-year period within the twenty-one-year course, there is only one week left until its end. From a providential perspective, this period originally extends until the end of April when the blessing ceremony was held. According to the number of years, it means that the teacher has walked through the entire twenty-one-year period. What has the teacher achieved that stands out after walking through the twenty-one-year course? Has he gathered more money than anyone who boasts of wealth in the world? Has he gained more power than anyone? Does he have more followers than anyone else? No matter how you look at it, he cannot be considered the best. 

In terms of numbers, when centered around thirty million, the groups of unification are certainly not large in number. So why is the Unification Church being questioned? It is because, over the past twenty years, while redeeming six thousand years of history, it has not fallen despite the trials and hardships, and it continues to live on a historical foundation. If it were to die, it would not be a problem. It is because it is alive that it becomes an issue. 

The fallen remnants may all rot away, but when those rotten remnants are used as fertilizer, new branches and buds will sprout from there. The newly sprouted branches and buds are similar to the reality of the joys and sorrows of six thousand years of history. As long as the main root does not die, even if the trunk is cut off, if it can draw sap from that root, it can rapidly grow new shoots in a short period. Do you understand what I mean? We will become that way. Thinking about this makes one feel good, doesn't it? 

Let’s say there is a big walnut tree. It has gone through storms and winds, and all its branches have broken, and even what remains has been burned. However, if the root is alive, when new shoots come out, if the burned trunk is cut off, those new shoots will spread out. Once they start to grow, they will spread uncontrollably. No one will be able to stop them. Do you all think so? "Yes." Then you should focus on that thought and act accordingly. 

Even if that tree grows vigorously, there is a limit to how much it can grow in essence. It cannot grow beyond that. Therefore, how large and thorough is the driving force that moves your heart? How deeply rooted are you, and how normally is your trunk growing? Depending on these factors, you can bring about results proportional to them, but when that driving force is faint, everything becomes vague. If that happens, it will end as a tree that bears no fruit. 

So what kind of driving force do you possess that aligns with such thoughts, like yeast? Ladies, grandmothers, what can be done if your hair has turned white? Even if your own hair has turned white, you must bring young people with black hair and educate them with that ideology. 

It seems that there are people here who have come from practicing the way on Mount Samgak, but those who have not practiced for more than three years should not be here. That means one must have a heart that exceeds the standard of having practiced for three years. 

In restoration, a central figure, a period, and conditions are needed. Did that lady over there come for the first time today? "Yes." She might be wondering if that person is the teacher, right? (Laughter) 

When we engage in our faith life or try to align our thoughts, we must center on the principles. Does anyone possess the motivation in their heart that can shake the world when they strike it, shake the land when they hit it, and break the heavens when they strike them? When God created the universe, did He think, "I will create it by pressing down tightly"? Would it work if He were a being without strength or ability? How could the earth come into being if a being without such power said, "Let the earth come into being"? 

Go to an oil mill and take a look. When you put sesame seeds into the oil press and apply pressure, sesame oil comes out. It must be pressed hard; if the pressing force is weak, it will not come out. Similarly, whether it is Korea or the world, or the three billion people of humanity, there must be a strong heart that is determined to pull them out, even if they crumble or break. One must not have a mindset that this is too great a task. 

You must first have knowledge of the theory, and then you must have the belief that it can be done. If your thoughts do not reach, and if your beliefs do not extend, it cannot become yours and is easily taken by others. However, the foundation that is solidified through your practice, the foundation that is firmly rooted, cannot be taken away unless greater strength and belief are applied. 

From this perspective, the trials that the Unification Church has gone through until now have been a necessary period to dig deep roots through a solid foundation, establishing an absolute foundation that no one can invade. 

So, is the seven-year period or the twenty-one-year period an important period or not? Is it an important period? If it is important, why is it important? It is because even Satan cannot handle this work that we are pushing forward and cannot block it; it is a period for establishing a solid foundation. The problem begins from here. The Unification Church believers who are rooted and growing here are like branches and leaves. Isn’t that right? But why do you all look so shabby? Three virtues of Christianity—obedience, submission, sacrifice. 

When I see you, I feel pity. You go to church and get beaten by your husbands, persecuted, and come to church looking completely wilted, so you deserve to be criticized. Look at your face in the mirror. Is your face one that can receive love from God? When the teacher tries to give you instructions, do you think, "Oh, what is the teacher trying to command now?" That sounds good, but in reality, it is frightening. Your insides are completely visible. Should I continue talking, or should I stop? "You should continue." What? Until the day I die? Saying I will talk for a thousand years until I die is nonsense. But should I continue this talk or not? It is nice to just listen. (Laughter) 

You must understand what the teacher means when he says to evangelize three people. What will happen in ten years? Should I hit you with a stick? Should I tell you to lie down and sleep? Should I tell you to jump down? Should I tell you to die? What do you think? Is it okay if I hit you, or if I tell you to jump down, or if I roll you over? "Yes." Oh, just words…. 

Are you going to get married? Then you will go, right? Even if it is not a good house? Then you will go, right? But that is just talk; where is the reality? 

When I gathered many brides and grooms of the Unification Church and asked them, they wanted to have a first-class handsome man as their husband, even though they had the ugliest faces. Once a woman marries and lives, she does not easily separate. If she separates after being bound, it becomes gossip all over the neighborhood. 

However, in the Unification Church, when they marry, it is not about meeting the bride and groom but forming a trinity centered on the father. The relationship between parents and children is prioritized over that of the bride and groom. Even after the ceremony, while the bride and groom might separate after a fight, the bond between father and children can never be severed. 

So, who is better off, the father who has good children, or the children who have a good father? Which is it? The children are the ones who have a good father. If the children are complete fools, how pitiful must that father be, who should be joyful about his children? 

God has found the sons and daughters He lost over six thousand years, but how must He feel seeing that the children He found after suffering for six thousand years are in such a state? When I think that I might have become someone who would lament, "It would have been better if I hadn't found them," after searching for six thousand years with a staff of suffering, do you have confidence in yourselves? 

When I reflect on those six thousand years, I must think about how I can treat the one and only father. There is no other way but to unconditionally obey him. That is how it is. 

That is why the religion that calls upon God must unconditionally obey Him. Isn’t that the etiquette that a person with a religion should have? Not only obedience but absolute submission is required. Not only submission but also sacrificing one’s life to become an offering. That is why Christianity teaches obedience, submission, and sacrifice. Therefore, it concludes that Christianity must be a true religion. 

For that reason, Christianity has become a religion of martyrdom, offering sacrifices to God and spreading the true meaning in this world. The fact that Christianity has truly become a global religion is due to this content. Do you understand? 

The issue is whether you are a seed that possesses vitality (driving force).

If you are the fruit of six thousand years, then the tree of six thousand years must have had both green and withered times. When the fruit ripens, what happens? The leaves dry up and fall off, and eventually, only the fruit remains. 

For the fruit to ripen, it must be autumn, and when it is autumn, the wind must blow. That wind is different from the summer wind. It is not a wind that can absorb trials from all environments or provide help by shielding everything; it is a wind that cleans and sucks out what has been covered. The wind that blows is a wind that makes everything negative, not positive. Such a wind must blow. 

When such truth, such principle, and such religion come forth, they must face the frost of the autumn season from the evil world. The teacher thinks that the Unification Church has faced that frost very well. Not only that, but the cold winter wind of Dong-samsak must blow, leaving only the bare branches. Even if the flesh of the fruit falls away during that process, there remains one seed hidden within that fruit. 

The true owner does not demand the fruit but demands the seed. The merchants dealing with orchards demand the flesh of the fruit, but the true owner demands the true seed within that fruit. 

Even if our Unification Church has endured countless hardships and has become a fruit hanging on bare branches, it is not about being pleased with the flesh of that fruit but about whether it has the seed within that fruit. This is the question. When the new spring comes in March, will that seed surely be born as a being with the vitality of the first fruit of the Unification Church? If that is not the case, it does not possess vitality. 

To possess vitality, the tree must go through all the storms and winds it must endure until it grows. It must have a history of trials. It must have the life force to pass through that harsh trial process and have hope for the future to welcome the new spring season, allowing new life to sprout. Thus, when summer passes and autumn arrives, it will become a seed with vitality.
Are you all like seeds? Not just like seeds, but do you have the natural driving force that can develop infinitely in the future, a force that no one can take away from you? The question is whether you have the driving force of life that can stimulate itself when a new era comes. Those who do not have that are like the dead. Things like seeds and fruits end up in a pile of fertilizer, do you understand?

Then why did the teacher say to gather only those who have been here for more than three years? It’s because you look like seeds, that is, you look like the seeds of the Unification Church. Even if you have gone through all kinds of hardships and your outer shell is wrinkled and rotten, as long as the seed hidden inside is good, that is all that matters. I asked you to gather those who have been here for more than three years because I want to plant such seeds.

You must become seeds that can sprout anywhere on this planet.

Purpose of the Seven-Year Course
What the teacher has worked hard for over the past seven years is to create such seeds. Even if the summer storms rage, the cold winds of autumn blow, and the snowstorms of winter strike, that is not the problem. After going through all that, seeds with even greater vitality must sprout.

What is the purpose of the 21-year course, or the seven-year course? It is to create the seeds of the Unification Church. You must become seeds that can plant the Unification Church itself within yourselves. Have you achieved that or not?

Until now, you have been swept away by the wind, running away in fear of storms. So, is it hanging on the tree or not? It is a leaf that has fallen from a broken branch. That is how you have lived until now. You have turned away from God and asked, “God, can you make history for me?”

When the teacher fought for 21 years, could we trigger the same connection that God had been cooperating behind the scenes to obtain the true seeds? From now on, even if the Unification Church is thrown into a new beginning, and even if stormy days come, can you grow as living beings that can trample all these harsh environments in place of the teacher? Are you able to do that?

You are like a fig tree without fruit. A fig tree without fruit is still alive. In fact, it is greener than a fruit-bearing tree. When you sleep, you go under the green tree without fruit, but when you eat, you go to the tree with fruit. Which is more precious? Is it more precious to eat or to sleep? Sleeping is more precious, isn’t it?

When I was in elementary school, I didn’t walk; I ran. I ran barefoot, without shoes. Was that a good time or is now better? Which time is better? But that is not the issue. The path we must take is the issue. A time when all your limbs and body can move according to your feelings and thoughts is a truly precious time. Has anyone felt such a time?

The issue is not how you have lived until now, but how you will live from now on. Within life itself, all feelings of harmony between heaven and earth must surround your heart. When you look at the flowing waves on a warm spring day, songs come out naturally, and the winter scenery with snow falling looks pitiful, but it feels like an absolutely necessary object for me. Is your heart like that too? Everyone has such poetic feelings. You should have a heart that is grateful for everything you see, knowing that there is nothing between you and others that is unrelated.

If the teacher were to push you away, where would you all go? What would happen if the teacher cut you off without knowing? When you think about this, when you have become a complete seed, it doesn’t matter how you act. However, when you are not, it becomes difficult.

Those of you who do not possess autonomy cannot enter the spiritual world. There is a world, a nation, a tribe, a family, and individuals in the spiritual world as well. From the perspective of the individual, heaven is a place you cannot enter without the autonomy to say, “I am absolutely necessary there.” Whether viewed from the perspective of the family or the tribe, you must have that kind of autonomy to say that you are absolutely necessary. Heaven is a place you can go only when you have that autonomy.

You must possess autonomy proportional to your corresponding position. If that position is high, you must establish absolute autonomy in your environment from a high standard; if it is low, you must establish it from a low standard. This characteristic is the personality given by God and the essence of individual truth.

Therefore, when you think about yourselves, are you perfect for your own individuality? Are you perfect for your family? Are you perfect for your tribe? Have you become the subject for everything that needs your existence before this country and this world?

What is necessary for strong faith?

Now, was the spring season until now passive or active? If it was a passive spring, how will you welcome an active spring? To welcome an active spring, you must become a complete seed. Why do we discuss God’s heart, God’s circumstances, and God’s wishes? This is not necessary in a passive position. However, since your individuality must break away from a passive environment at some point and establish an active environment, you cannot avoid discussing it.

To be active, it is not enough to have only God’s heart. You must connect God’s wishes, heart, and circumstances from reality to the future. Only then can you start with a new subjectivity centered on the historical stage of reality. That is where you finally establish a victorious foundation.

Centered on God, the subject of the universe and the subject of heaven, the heart of God and the circumstances and wishes of God become the issues that have passed through the historical era.

In a passive position, if there is no subject, Satan will always attack. When there is no active subject, Satan is always in an attacking posture. When attacked by Satan, the question is whether you will be shattered and destroyed or not, and it cannot be done by individuals alone. That is why faith companions are necessary. Jesus also went through the three years of public life centered on the twelve disciples as companions in faith, but in the end, he had to connect them through the relationship of sharing his sacrifice. That is why faith companions are necessary. Why? To block many enemies when they come to attack. After that, faith children are needed. Why? To dream of happiness in my family life and to lay the foundation for new life.

To seek faith companions
