The second seven-year course of activity  
In the second seven-year course, both those who came first and those who came later must go. The first comers might say, "We have already gone through the first seven-year course, so we don't need to go through the second." But that is not in accordance with principle.  
The teacher tried to establish a foundation and start through the seven-year course, but it did not happen, so it was extended to 21 years. You may not know well, but now that the time has come closer, even if you cannot go, you must go through the second seven-year course. If that happens, we will enter a time of establishing the basis for the hope of Jesus, who longed for the return of Israel.  
When I ask if you have the heart to go with such feelings, there are not many people like that. Fortunately, many people think that they can just come to see the teacher like this, but those people are not in the position of the owner; they are in the position of a guest. They are not in the position of the owner.  
Therefore, you must now resolve to quietly start the second seven-year course with the appearance of having the attributes of eternity and prepare for this path ahead.  
Until now, our Unification Church has only done external work. So what should the Unification Church do from now on? This is the question. While it is important to lay the ideological foundation and move forward, it is also extremely important how we conduct our practical lives.  
What should our Unification Church do in the future? We must engage in business. Until now, we have run barefoot and received insults, but now we must also establish a social foundation to earn a true seed and solve economic issues.  
So what kind of business will we engage in to establish such a social living foundation? That is the question. Until now, we have mobilized everyone, regardless of age or gender, to the front lines. That was unavoidable because our church was in an emergency. However, now that we have reached a point where we can go beyond that limit, we must adopt a dual strategy. In other words, it is now time to prepare the rear.  
For the front line to succeed, we must establish supply routes. To continuously secure these supply routes, we must develop supply depots. We must prepare all economic conditions necessary for the military centered around these supply depots. We cannot overlook these issues.  
Now we have entered an era where we need both the first and second fronts. While ordinary people can earn money and live their personal lives, we are different. Those who work in the second responsibility department must earn money not for themselves but for those working on the front line. Until now, we have engaged in a war of attrition, but in the future, we must establish supply routes to support what is needed for the front line soldiers. This era is coming upon us. The time of suffering and starving while enlightening is now over.  
So what kind of Unification Church will we become? What should we do? "We must earn money." If we earn money, how will we earn it? You need to understand this broadly. In the future, we must divide those who can take normal responsibility for the development of our church from those who cannot and establish a rear economic system. Therefore, the plan is to establish factories in each district and regional unit.  
Economic foundation construction plan  
Currently, our country is promoting the second five-year economic development plan. We must align ourselves with that and create our sub-factories in 150 regions centered around 8 districts for our internal foundation. This is the teacher's plan. To do this, we need to import everything from abroad, but it requires enormous capital, making it impossible. We do not have such capital. Therefore, the teacher's plan and thought is to prepare it in place.  
So in 1968, we need to secure at least 150 machines centered around the Sutaek-ri factory. Along with this, about 300 machines need to be equipped. Therefore, in 1968, we must produce at least 120 machines. This is an absolutely necessary quantity to meet the target we planned for 1969. Without producing this, we will not be able to manufacture many machines in the future. Currently, looking at the 150 regions, if we install at least 10 machines in each place and operate them well, there will be considerable development in the future.  
Looking at the example of Cheonggyecheon 4-ga, just three years ago, when people running small factories asked other factories for something, they would come directly to take orders. However, now even if they go to order, they cannot produce the required quantity immediately, so they must make a reservation and come back after a few months. What does this indicate? It shows that the current industry in Korea has not developed significantly in a flat manner, and the technological foundation is still lacking.  
In light of this, Korea is now in a position where it must develop in all fields for about the next 15 years. Therefore, we must seize this period well and revive economically. So if we experiment for about three years starting this year, it will surely succeed. To create these sub-factories centered around each regional headquarters, we need 1,800 machines. To produce 1,800 machines over three years, we must produce 600 machines a year. This means we need to produce about 2 machines on average per day.  
We expect the price of the lathes we will produce and sell in the future to be around 400,000 won. The Sutaek-ri factory must be equipped to produce more than 2 machines a day. Additionally, planning for future market sales, we should be able to produce an average of more than 3 or 4 machines.  
To do this, we need to establish internal facilities. Therefore, we must quickly prepare the basic factory facilities to install the machines produced in our factory at local sub-factories. Of course, the products we are currently producing must also be made according to certain specifications.  
Currently, our factory has reached a level where it can produce anything, even foreign products. Originally, the teacher planned for three years, but it has reached that level in just a year and eight months. The current state of our factory is different from that of other general factories. The people who come to our factory know nothing about machines. In general factories, people who do not know how to handle machines must work for more than three years to be entrusted with machines worth hundreds of thousands of won, but in our factory, they are entrusted from the day they arrive. Therefore, while it takes about five years to acquire technology in a general factory, it takes only six months in our factory. What does this show? It shows that people who have worked for more than three years in general factories are now working in our factory, and there is no problem in catching up with their level.  
There is a particularly difficult process in making machines. We must overcome this regardless. Whether it takes a year or several years, we must get over this hurdle. Without doing so, we cannot keep up with the global standard in the future. That is why the teacher instructed the original department to disassemble and verify all American and Japanese machines or other important machines. We must know which of those machines are superior and which are not. This is one of the favorable methods for us to quickly acquire technology in our factory.  
Therefore, it takes a year to make a machine that could be made in a year, but it takes a year and a half. Why is that? It is because we must cultivate the technology to overcome all local difficulties or to handle all machines necessary for that, and we do not simply pass through but verify everything precisely. Japanese and American lathes and all machines are quite precise. We must also be able to manufacture such machines. In fact, the lathes we have are better than American ones. Now we can do in a year and eight months what would normally take three years. So now we must have someone responsible for the production enterprise.  
Efficiency and mental strength  
Currently, our production manager has a genius quality. He was a driver but is very good at designing and knows how to do everything. He can understand any complex machine just by looking at it once. This time, he went to Japan and visited several important large factories that are among the top ten, and he saw a lot. He made all of that into a catalog and concluded that our factory can produce all of those things as well. Therefore, the teacher's plan is to create a factory with such a system in a rapid timeframe.  
He plans to create 150 such factories within three years, and it costs about 3.5 to 4 million won to create one factory. He intends to do this from our capital from the very beginning. He plans to do this within three and a half to four years, and during that period, our factory will definitely not go bankrupt.  
You do not need to worry that the machines made in our factory will not sell. Since they will be sent to our factory after production, the items will run out, and there will be no surplus.  
Therefore, we must first cultivate excellent technicians. So when we create 150 factories, we must have a system that can produce dozens of lathes a day in our factory. Considering the current situation in Korea and looking ahead to the Korean industrial sector, we will be able to stand at the forefront of the Korean industrial sector without any problems.  
We can produce machines that are qualitatively superior to hundreds of large factories. Why is that? In general factories, if they set a production target of 1,000 machines a year while paying salaries to technicians, they must produce 80 machines a month. Therefore, the workers there do not pay attention to quality just to meet the required quantity. They think that as long as they produce and receive their salaries, it does not matter what happens to the owner. That is why they skip over difficult processes. As a result, the quality of the products becomes terrible. The mindset of those working in that way is incomparable to ours. Furthermore, because we are united, if it takes them 100 hours to make one machine, we can reduce that to between 50 and 70 hours. The teacher experimented with this recently. Until now, the quantity of machines we produced was only one-third of the target, but when all the workers united and worked with one heart, we were able to increase productivity by more than three times. This shows how great the human spirit can be.  
Looking at this, I believe we will easily surpass the planned numbers. By 1968, we must produce the planned quantity of lathes no matter what. The plan to have more than 300 lathes is to support the economy of local churches.  
So what will we do with the profits left over from here? That money does not belong to the teacher. It belongs to the district leaders who have worked the hardest among those who have put in effort until now, and the regional leaders who have worked the hardest among them. We must use it to solve the economic issues of those who have worked the hardest to establish the tradition of our church.  
Looking at the nationwide situation, there are currently 1,700 myeons. In the future, our church must also prepare basic agricultural land that can farm centered around the district church units. Therefore, we are trying to launch the agricultural cooperative that is currently being built.  
In this agricultural cooperative, we will bring in all the young people who have entered our cause and provide agricultural guidance. We will prepare at least 4,000 to 5,000 pyeong of farmland to teach them farming.  
And we must create a rice mill. Rural people do not know how machines work when they are suddenly brought to a factory. So we will operate the rice mill with our members. We will gather all the young people who are idle during the farming off-season and buy all the rice from the entire village and large farms, then mill it and sell it. This way, we will be farming twice.  
Young people with talent will operate the rice mill engine. After working for a year like this, they will learn how machines operate. Once they endure that year, they will become interested, thinking, "Ah, this is what is made in the factory!" So the rice mill will become an intermediate process. If we operate the rice mill locally in this way, our economic issues can be resolved without money. It means that we can eat wherever we go.  
We have favorable conditions for laying an economic foundation  
If we mobilize just three people from each of the 1,700 myeons, that makes 5,100 people, right? These people will eat and do this work every day. If that happens, we will not have to worry about where to eat. Once this economic foundation is established, we can engage many people in public activities at any time.  
If ten people farm and produce enough food for twenty people to eat for a year, that is immense. Then, even if we assign twenty people to one myeon every day, we can operate without money. We must establish such an economic base.  
In the future, our factory cannot help but become a global factory. Once we surpass a certain standard, we will bring our members from Japan to work in the factory.
Yes. Also, in about three years, not only Japanese but also excellent technicians from the United States and Germany will all be deployed to our factory. Since our ideologies are unified, whether they are American, German, or Japanese technicians, they are all our technicians. We will call those technicians to integrate the world's renowned technological systems and focus on the development of a factory in Korea.

Looking at all economic activities in each country now, it is an era where everyone secretly keeps their own secrets and employs industrial spies to turn others' assets into their own. However, no matter how much we try, we cannot compete with that. In the coming years, we are preparing to pioneer markets in Southeast Asia before Japan does. In both domestic and international competition, we have various advantages. Therefore, we want to create machines similar to those of the invading country, Japan, and face them once. Then, we will establish mission departments in each country, and since we will have already paved the way for markets that are difficult for the local people to develop, we will not be able to be matched in the future.

The issue is how Korea will establish a global economic foundation centered around Japan. From now on, we need money, so we must earn money. In the future, I plan to establish a department store in Japan. I will send five or six executives from Korea there to open formal transactions with Japan.

Currently, when we order any machinery from Japan, it takes about a year to a year and a half. The reason is that in the past, Koreans and Japanese were enemies, and Japanese people do not trust Koreans. Recently, the head of the Japanese business department visited Korea and stopped by the Japanese embassy, where the embassy staff said that all Koreans are scammers and should never be trusted. They think all Koreans are scammers.

In this situation, even if a Korean entrepreneur asks to borrow machinery to establish a factory, the Japanese will not lend it. Therefore, to start trading with the Japanese, one must go in person to persuade them and provide evidence documents that they can trust. Only after they conduct a field investigation and can believe it will they nod in agreement.

However, we are starting from Korea with a Japanese organization. If we set up a trading company in Japan and prepare a budget in Korea, we will not waste a year or incur travel costs. If we just make a phone call from here, within three hours, actual operational members will be dispatched nationwide. Our organization in Japan is structured that way. No capable person in Korea can follow such an organization. If we order machinery here, what would take a year and a half will be brought directly by a Japanese person within a few months. This is because our church in Japan guarantees it.

The way we live, the work that only we can do
Japan is currently experiencing overproduction and is competing to find markets. Because of this situation, as long as the Japanese church takes responsibility and guarantees, we can bring in as much machinery as we want. In Japan, they offer payment plans from 18 months to 2 years, but we can extend it to 3 years. Since we will be bringing in products in bulk, companies are scrambling to receive orders. Therefore, if we bring products from Japan on a payment plan and sell them in cash in Korea, we can pay back the principal with just the interest from that money and still make a profit.

And we are faster than anyone else. While others have to wait a year and a half to receive goods, once we establish our foundation, we can export products that Japan was planning to export to other countries. 

To do this, we will attach unique identification numbers to all goods exported from Japan to foreign countries and prepare two copies of a catalog, keeping one copy at the company here. Then, when we receive an order through our organization in Japan, we just need to send a telegram to match the product's number and request the shipment. Then, the goods will be transported to the importing country, and we will earn intermediary profits. This is how a person without money can make money.

If this works well between Korea and Japan, we will also do it between Korea and the United States, and between Korea and Germany. We will also do it between Germany and the United States, the United States and Japan, and Germany and Japan. To expand our global market, we need to prepare from now on. Do you understand? "Yes."

In the future, when our followers increase globally, we must help each other live. When that time comes, we will create a tailor shop so that all Unification Church members do not go elsewhere to get their suits but have them made at our tailor shop. Collaborating like that is the way we live, and it is something only we can do.

In the future, I plan to make Korea an international industrial nation. We will produce cars and machinery. Given this plan, what will the Unification Church do in the future? We will industrialize Korea. To do that, we need to establish sub-factories and develop them. In the future, we will send excellent foreign technicians to Korea and assign specialized technicians to the precise machinery of those factories so that each factory can produce a unique product. This way, we can produce machinery in 150 special categories, which is my vision. Thus, we aim to rapidly advance Korea's industrial technology.

We will also guide scientific farming methods and practically train local practitioners. We must realize scientific farming in Korea's rural areas no matter what. We will start this from now on. Do you understand? "Yes."

Until now, we have all served others. However, from now on, we must operate factories to organize our system and lay the foundation for our economy. This is the future operational plan that you must understand. Therefore, the wives and family members should start praying from now on. In the future, I will place all the blessed families that I have blessed in every village. And all the women will live in the main family house. They must serve with loyalty until their bones break to restore that lineage. Until now, we have conducted external operations, but from now on, we must develop internal operations centered around our own lineage. If only the blessed people can solve economic issues, all problems will be easily resolved.

The purpose of economic restoration
Korea must bring in foreign capital in the future. That is why I am trying to create a wave now. We want to establish standards that foreign people will find acceptable enough to invest and form technological partnerships.

So how will we create 150 factories in three years? We will do everything on a payment plan from abroad. We will repay in installments over five months. For the initial factory setup, we only need to pay about 500,000 to 600,000 won in cash for raw materials and operating funds. If the factory runs well for a year and a half, it can get on the right track.

What will this factory do in the future? It will produce parts for large general factories. By entrusting us, they will gain the credibility that their planned designs are accurate. Then, large factories will wonder how we can produce such good parts with the technology and equipment we have, even though our factory has only recently been established. This way, our factory will surely be able to sustain itself. We will utilize the sub-factories in the field as promotional outposts to develop our market. Since our product quality is good, once they use it, they will recognize it. Thus, in the future, we will surely be able to sell our machines wherever machinery is being installed.

By doing this, starting from 1970, three years later, we will expand our machinery installation and begin mass production. Then, no foreign machines will be sold in Korea. We also plan to start working on automatic machinery installations from next year, and after about three years of preparation, we will be on the right track. Therefore, we must prepare an automatic equipment system from now on for the next 7 to 8 years. We need to lay a solid foundation in this field that no one can follow, design a process that can actually produce, and advance our work. Therefore, when I start making money, I will not leave you who have worked hard behind. Even with just the money that foreign people help us with, we will have enough to live on. Just wait and see if that’s true or not. I will take responsibility for the hardships I have put you through.

The living expenses for the regional leaders in 150 areas can be covered with 300,000 won a year. With 15,000 won a month, many people can live, so even with just the interest from that money, they can survive. While it is not ideal to live off interest, providing about 500,000 won a year is not a problem. 

And we want to create farmland in each region. If we calculate 4,000 pyeong of land at 200 won per pyeong, that amounts to 800,000 won, and with 1,700 districts, it totals 1.36 billion won. For establishing our factory, we can clearly buy land at 163 won per pyeong. By doing this, it seems like I am definitely becoming a businessman. (Laughter) We want to gather young people during the off-season and give it a try. Whether it succeeds or fails, we will try. A pipe-cutting machine costs 500,000 won, so even if the machine incurs additional costs, we will do it centered around God. In the past, we managed to cut down what would take other factories weeks or months to process in just a week.

In the future, what will the Unification Church be known for? It will be a place that manages factories rather than just business. Currently, in Japan, they produce a lot but have no market. Now is the time to develop this market through global activities.

I plan to bless about 430 couples this time. Centered around these brides and grooms, about 3,200 parents will be mobilized, and if we include the brides and grooms, it will be about 4,000 people. There are about 800 families of the brides and grooms, and if we include their extended families, it could be around 400,000. (Laughter) They will not receive any support for gathering together for a joint wedding of Unification Church members, but there will be a lot of interest, and they will spread the word around the neighborhood. As that happens, people's interest in which bachelor will marry which maiden in the Unification Church joint wedding will grow significantly.

Will the local young men and women just sit still? They will be excited and swarm around like bees, dancing day and night, and it will probably be amazing. 

As the rumors spread, it is likely that each bride and groom will be connected to about a thousand people. If they all gather in Seoul and hold hands, what will happen? It will be 4 million people. Just for their daily meals and lodging, it will amount to 400,000 won, which is a significant number. They have their mothers and fathers, and their maternal grandparents, right? They also have their father's siblings, sisters, and brothers-in-law, right? All of these connections matter. When they opposed the Unification Church, all their extended families opposed it too, but now they will gather out of interest and restoration.

This is just for 400 couples, but think about what will happen when we hold a joint wedding for about 4,000 couples in the future. It could involve around 40 million people. At that rate, there won't be many Koreans left. (Laughter)

The 430 couples' blessing to restore 4,300 years of national history
The 430 couples' blessing we will receive after the first seven-year course is to restore our 4,300 years of history. It also fulfills the 430 years it took for the Israelite nation to return from Egypt to Canaan during the restoration course. Therefore, by January 15 of next year, we will complete the 430 couples in three phases.

Then, what will happen in the future? If a family receives a bride from the Unification Church, that household will prosper in all matters. Even if they appear small and insignificant like a pumpkin, no one in the past has received a daughter-in-law with such loyalty, passion, and ethics. We aim to have such a devoted eldest daughter-in-law. You all must do this for three years.

In the future, we will create family visiting teams to visit each household. When we go to their homes, we will say we are from the Unification Church and are here to check if they are managing their household well. We will ask, "How is your daughter-in-law?" and we must not hear anything negative.

If this happens, all the local grandparents, parents, and children will say they want to join the Unification Church, and the young women will want to marry into the Unification Church. As we create this environment, parents who used to beat their children for wanting to join the Unification Church will instead beat them for not wanting to join. (Laughter) This way, the living foundation will be completely established. This is the strategy I will implement.

This year, if the young men and women want to get married, they must complete the 430 couples. Seven years is a traditional number, so if we do not reach 430 couples, I will not arrange marriages. From now on, we will be busy day and night to complete the 430 couples! (Laughter) We must be able to complete the 430 couples within this year. Is that right? We cannot afford to do worse than last year! So if you do not want to get married, do not evangelize. There is a tradition to uphold.

I will bless 36 families, 72 families, 120 families, and established families centered around the seven-year course and bless 430 families. From these approximately 1,000 families, we can expect to have around 50 smart babies born each year, right? (Laughter)

What is interesting this time is that the young men are running around like bees. They probably cannot sleep or work in their hometowns, but they are staying up all night wondering what is going on. This time, the young men who used to enjoy barley rice in the countryside are now sitting on the floor for days, and they feel like they are dying.

In the future, we will provide minimum living assistance to the blessed families. When they go out to evangelize, it used to be common to eat three or four meals a week and go hungry for three or four days, but they should at least eat porridge three times a day. In the future, we will provide minimum living assistance, so all blessed family members should enter the factories. If you fall behind now, you will have nowhere to go. We will train you to be able to work as responsible leaders and educate the local factory employees. Now, we must work hard to earn a living and live well.

Let’s become givers instead of takers
We must absolutely not live in debt. If I live in debt, I will not live in debt. Can we achieve unification while living in debt? Those who live in debt will perish. Therefore, we must never be in debt, no matter where we go. You must work as hard as you can.
You must leave behind what is necessary for the public good and become a person who can give and share. Those who take and leave without giving are robbers and thieves. Communists say that if you don't want to work, you shouldn't eat. However, we must eat for ourselves and also feed others. In the future, we must help the miserable people living around Africa and Southeast Asia. Our church is considering providing foreign aid as well. If our church provides aid to foreign countries, what will happen? Until now, our Korean church has not been able to provide aid to foreign countries. From now on, you must become the arms and legs, struggling and pushing forward. Do you understand? "Yes." The teacher has faced numerous opposition to build this factory, but he is thinking that far ahead. Therefore, we must divide into first and second lines and lay a self-sufficient foundation. Until now, we have learned God's heart through tears and sweat, but now we must lay an economic foundation. To restore the world, a global economic foundation is necessary.

That is why the teacher intends to manage the factory. Why is that? It is to put in effort. Making money is important, but we must put in effort beyond just making money. We should put in effort to a standard that heaven and earth can recognize, one that cannot be exchanged for a fortune. We must gather all the wealth of heaven through that effort.

If one puts in effort with a desire for material wealth, they are a thief. You should go to the factory early in the morning and put in effort. What happens if you don't? The teacher says you must enter the factory to meet him. Is the teacher the owner of the factory? However, since no one can work well, the teacher has no choice but to intervene. If the children cannot do it, can you? It is said that they have given birth to useless children. Still, having children is better than not having any. (Laughter) Even if you give birth to a child who is clumsy or foolish, it is still better than having none.

So how will we supplement this deficiency? Is there no way? You have all worked hard until now, but I think you need to work even harder. Is that a bad feeling or a good feeling? "Good." With a heart of apology, we must close our eyes and make them work. So, we will embark on the seven-year course again.

In the future, there will come a time when it will be easier for you to evangelize. Many students will gather around the principle study group, saying they want to study the teachings of Teacher Moon of the Unification Church. If that happens, if the teacher takes them for just one year and educates them, they will completely change and bow their heads. After that, all those who are capable will be brought in to pull the cart, farm, and sweat and dedicate themselves to saving this country, which is the teacher's thought.

Knowing this, you must exert all your strength until that time comes. And as we prepare to start again next year, I hope you will make a resolution for activity and take time to reflect on yourselves at home and pray earnestly.

Have all the things the teacher wanted to do this year been accomplished? This is not about me wanting to live well. It is all to prepare for your tomorrow.

<Prayer> Father, there are many who praise your holy name on this earth, and many who claim to be your beloved sons and daughters, but how many among them can truly open their hearts and share their circumstances with you? The more I think about it, the more I feel the sorrowful reality.

Father, I thank you for remembering this poor nation that has been chased among countless peoples and lands, and for choosing this lonely land of the Korean Peninsula to establish the focus of your providence. The thought that a group capable of being faithful to this will is exceedingly precious makes me feel even more ashamed. However, when I think that your heart of love is more with the disabled child than with the perfect child, I hope you will forgive this nation, which has a historical background that makes you worry.

Father, the children of unification have walked a history of painful struggle for seven years, hidden from others. Sometimes they have been oppressed, sometimes they have wept and lamented, and sometimes they have embraced their hungry bellies while discussing your circumstances, shedding endless tears.

Although all past events began with tears, the fact that they can be harvested not with tears but with laughter and can express gratitude before you is all due to your help and protection, and for that, I cannot help but be more grateful.

We sincerely hope that a world of freedom will soon be realized where we can freely express our desires to boast before you. We earnestly wish that you will accept all our stories as we bow down and worship before you.

Father, today is a holy day. Please listen to the earnest hearts of your lonely children scattered throughout South Korea, looking towards this place with their knees bent. When we have sad circumstances and come to you, please comfort them with the same love you have shown us as a friend and protector.

No matter what anyone says, we are lonely people without possessions. You alone are on our side, you alone are ours, and we must be those who know that living for you is a precious fact that cannot be exchanged for a fortune in this world, so I earnestly hope that their hearts will not be disappointed.

In Seoul, there is the headquarters of unification connected to the world. Please remember your children who remain here. We know that this place can be a fearful place, a sad place, and a difficult place. However, if we are a group that lives in you, can communicate with you, and lives through you, then we know that you will forever dwell in the place where we stand, directly overseeing and governing our lives, and for that, we are even more grateful for the grace that has allowed us to stand here.

Father, we are unworthy, but we sincerely thank you for allowing us to stand in this position today due to the foundation of righteousness built by our ancestors throughout their lives and the benefits of the times. Please allow this heart of gratitude to be one that is not just for myself but also for the historical perspective through the past, present, and future. I know that such a victorious figure will be recognized by you as a more valuable existence than any historical figure, so I earnestly hope and wish to be placed in such a position.

Father! Now we are about to welcome the new year of 1968, so may all the heavenly programs you plan for this year be completed, and may the kingdom you desire be realized on this earth, allowing us to raise the banner of victory and return honor, glory, and praise to you, making it a joyful year.

Father, may all your children connected by heart become brothers who can draw out your heart. I earnestly hope that they will be your sons and daughters who can establish a lineage of hope through the relationship between faithful parents and faithful children.

Please remember all your children scattered throughout the world. Even today, there are many who are fighting in lonely places centered on your heart, so I earnestly hope that you will remember them.

Until we meet again, please protect us personally, and may we be those who pledge and resolve to leave behind a heavenly loyalty that fulfills your wishes for our entire lives.

As we welcome the new year and embark on the second seven-year course, may we be able to make a new resolution and move forward boldly through the words we have heard. Even in places where fierce storms are blowing, heaven has achieved victory, so if we firmly resolve to follow in that path, we know that the way will be shortened and smooth, so I earnestly ask that we be allowed to be children who can take strong steps into the second seven-year course with new resolutions as we welcome the new year.

I earnestly ask that your grace and the glory of victory be with us in all things, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

**Position and Mission of Blessed Families**
<Summary of the Message> Blessing is God's wish and the wish of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. This wish must be fulfilled for a new history to open. The blessing is to fulfill this overall wish. Therefore, blessed families must be able to stand as the subjects that fulfill this wish.

Jesus could not fulfill this wish, which is why he must return to accomplish it. The Unification Church must take responsibility for fulfilling the wish that Jesus could not achieve. Until the blessing is fulfilled, we must resolve the grievances spanning the three generations of Adam, Jesus, and the Lord of the Second Advent. Establishing the external foundation that Jesus could not establish is precisely the seven-year course.

The teacher's wedding ceremony must be more grand than any wedding ceremony to date, but it could not be grand due to the suffering endured. Therefore, conditions remain to make it grand in the future.

Members must stand in the position of having the best marriage externally among the three generations centered on themselves. Only then can conditions be set before Satan. That is why we hold the joint wedding ceremony. To have a marriage that pleases God internally, we must establish material conditions.

We must pay a restoration fund to indemnify the fact that Jesus could not find and establish the twelve disciples. Therefore, we must provide a sacrificial condition of 30,000 won corresponding to twelve people and three numbers. By doing so, we will stand in the position of having established the largest condition in the world.

December 26, 1967 (Tuesday), Daejeon Church.

The foundation of internal victory will be established according to the results of spiritual victory.

However, the problem is that blessed families do not establish traditions. Because they could not practice the teacher's guidance, before the first seven-year course ends, we must make the second arrangement to establish this period as suitable before God.

The 33 families were also established after establishing three families.

The character of a person is determined by how many will shed tears at their death.

Through the death of baby Hye-jin, I felt God's heart in losing Jesus and realized that I have not yet been loyal enough before God to escape death.

**Stand as a Tribal Messiah**
<Summary of the Message> It is important for us to penetrate the established church and secure God's human resources.

The blessing means the True Parents and True Children coming together to fulfill the purpose of creation. A person with a national fortune will not perish even if familial misfortunes come. Likewise, a person with a global fortune will never perish even if faced with national or ethnic misfortunes.

An Abel family cannot stand before God without establishing a Cain family. Jacob also could not stand in the position of Abel without turning the results of his 21 years of labor over to Esau and establishing Esau before God.

The first seven-year course is a period to create tribal messiahs, to take children away from the world of Satan and bless them. The following seven-year course is a period to return to the family with the mission of the Messiah.

Thus, we will restore God's first and second blessings. However, the material world must restore the three numbers. Restoring these three numbers is precisely the restoration of all things, that is, the restoration of the economy.

December 27, 1967 (Wednesday), Daejeon Church.

**Let Us Establish the World of Heart**
<Summary of the Message> The standards we have worked and acted upon during the seven-year course surpass the standards of anyone who has labored throughout the 6,000 years of history.

**Goals of the Seven-Year Course**
Looking at the current international situation in the world, which is in an apocalyptic era, we can see that this is a more important time than ever. In such times, we must recognize that our responsibility to establish internal standards regarding the visible external world is greater than ever. We are living in a crucial time that cannot be exchanged even for the 6,000 years of history.

However, among us, there are those who think that once the seven-year course passes, something great will happen, and this world of Satan will suddenly turn to God's side.

So what is our goal during the seven-year course? Of course, the ultimate goal is to restore the entire world and build the kingdom of heaven, but even more urgent is the task of determining the center.

Once a perfect center, that is, a perfect subject is determined, a perfect object will arise.

It is a matter of the principle. In terms of electricity, just as a complete positive charge generates a complete negative charge in front of it, and a complete negative charge generates a complete positive charge in front of it, this is the same principle. 
When we say that the world today is at an end, it means that, centered on God, the heavenly fortune is being driven into the era of negativity (-). The era of negativity is akin to the fortune of the satanic world. As heavenly fortune comes to this earth, in the end, the era of negativity, that is, the satanic world, will collapse. Right now is a time of confusion. 
If we view today as heavenly fortune, it is the time when the era of negativity is arriving. As the era of negativity gradually enters into a realm where it can be completed, a complete positive (+) form will also emerge. Therefore, when unity occurs in the external world, unity will also occur in the internal world. 
From this perspective, the vertical purpose of the seven-year course is to determine the center. This center can represent heaven and can also represent the world, nations, ethnic groups, families, and individuals. The center that represents all of this is one. No matter how great an existence may be, in order to establish a decisive position as an existence, it must connect with the standard of this center. A period of seven years is necessary to determine this central standard. 
Looking at the history of the providence of restoration, God brings forth the entire global fortune. God created the vast universe in the beginning and established Adam and Eve at its center. When creating Adam and Eve, He made them with all the elements of creation and endowed them with many things, among which the most important is heart. When this heart becomes completely one, the ideal of creation that God desired when He created the entire universe will be fulfilled, and that is the realization of the four-position foundation. The center of the four-position foundation is heart, and the core of the four-position foundation is love. The most fundamental point of all existence is heart. 
Then how are love and heart different? When we talk about love, we usually feel a fluttering emotion, while heart seems to be closely related to the mind. However, heart has a four-dimensional nature. Therefore, heart becomes more central to the whole than love. Heart is like the resultant position that has gone through the process of love. Thus, heart becomes the center of the three-dimensional world. Therefore, our Unification Church has been advocating to establish a world of heart rather than a world of love until now. 
In this way, the center of everything is heart, and this heart must be centered on the family and must rise up. Such a heart must be connected and united centered on God. At this time, the united heart must become one not only individually but also as a family, nation, country, and world. 
From this perspective, the completion of restoration cannot be without heart. This is because the position of the center cannot be established without it. 
The fortune that the Unification Church aims for 
Completion is possible from the standard where a perfect center is determined. In order to be completed, the center of the universe, world, nation, ethnic group, family, and individual must be determined, and all of this must be heart. It is impossible to achieve completion without going through heart. 
Individually, salvation occurs when the mind and body become one and align in action. Thus, centered on the individual, the family is saved, and based on that family, the ethnic group is saved, and thus the nation, country, and world are saved. 
What is the highest purpose of the seven-year course? It is to lay the foundation of heart that can represent the whole in front of the providence of restoration. 
The reason we have walked the seven-year course until now is to love God. To love God means to stand in a position of oneness with God. In that position, when we possess a heart that is in harmony with God and care for the nation and the world, we stand in a position that represents God. 
Therefore, the regions we are currently assigned to in our external activities are not merely areas belonging to a certain county. That place is a central point where the world and heaven are connected. Thus, each person must represent God, serve God, and learn with a heart that is in harmony with God. Our central goal during the seven-year course has been to understand God's circumstances and fulfill God's desires. 
We have thought of God's desires and have left behind our blood, sweat, and tears. We have held onto our family members, shedding blood, sweat, and tears over God's circumstances. This is because, centered on our heart's connection, the world can be connected and revived; that is, heart can be connected. Thus, when we crush Satan in that position and escape from the place where Satan accuses, that environment will return to heaven. We have promoted such work. 
Until now, the results of our struggle against the nation indicate that the time when this ethnic group opposed us has passed. Here, one thing you must understand is that there is individual fortune, and there is also family, ethnic, national, and world fortune. If so, what kind of fortune does the Unification Church aim for? It is not the fortune that any ethnic group, nation, or world aims for. It is the fortune that heaven aims for. 
In order to lead this fortune well, personal fortune must be corrected and managed on a global scale. Heavenly fortune is for the purpose of managing the world, so in order to align with that heavenly fortune, one must possess personal fortune that can represent global standards. A family must also be a family that can represent the world in order to occupy the fortune of a global family. An ethnic group must also be an ethnic group that can represent many ethnic groups in the world to access the fortune of a global ethnic group, and the same goes for nations and the world. 
The limits of heavenly fortune and the seven-year course

Thus, when we connect with heavenly fortune, it will return, and we can connect to the center of that returning fortune. Then we can ride on heavenly fortune from the relative position of that center. 
The reason we do this is to avoid destruction. If we do not do this, we will perish. No matter how capable an individual may be, if the family collapses, that individual will also experience a fortune of collapse. An individual cannot prevent the fortune of a collapsing family with their own fortune. If a family has ten members, one cannot block the fortune of ten family members with their own fortune. Similarly, one cannot block the fortune of the world with the fortune of a nation. 
Therefore, in order not to perish before heavenly fortune, we must not enter the realm of fortune that has been spoken of in the world until now. We must escape from the realm of worldly fortune and align ourselves with heavenly fortune. 
The national fortune through heavenly fortune, the ethnic fortune through national fortune, the family fortune through ethnic fortune, and the personal fortune through family fortune must all align with the fortune based on heavenly fortune. 
Then, what does heavenly fortune revolve around? It revolves around God. Then, what does God revolve around? He revolves around His heart, circumstances, desires, and purpose. Such a person has entered into the realm of fortune that connects from the individual to heaven, so they will not perish in any era. 
The purpose of your activities over the past seven years has been to ride on heavenly fortune. Until now, Satan has been blocking heavenly fortune. We had to resolve what was caught, and if we were to be sacrificed to Satan and disappear as offerings of evil, we must completely strip away the resentment left behind and the yoke imposed on all of humanity that has succumbed to Satan. Today's Christians are unaware of the tremendous mission that Jesus had. They simply believe that if they have faith, they will go to heaven. How simple is that? 

If there was something that Jesus longed for in His heart, what would it have been? It was to go forth as a victorious prince before God and inherit God's full authority on earth. To do this, He had to establish a lineage recognized by God in the positions of family, nation, and world within the realm of God's love. 

This is not something that can be accomplished easily. So what must be done? He must completely indemnify all that Adam and Eve fell into, and all the resentment left before God by their fallen descendants throughout history, in order to stand in the position of the ancestor who establishes the new Israel, and finally appear in the position of true parents, starting anew centered on God's love. 

Humans can only receive heavenly inheritance by serving in the position of those parents. This is the feast of the Lamb of God. In other words, one must go through the position of blessing spoken of in today's Unification Church. This means receiving blessings from God. 

Because Adam and Eve, that is, God's only son and daughter, fell, the blood of love became defiled, and it must be cleansed centered on God's love. We must boldly block Satan, who has been accusing and presenting conditions for offerings throughout history. Thus, we must determine the position of the perfect only son and daughter who can enter the glorious world where only God intervenes. Without going through this blessed position, one cannot embark on the path of restoration toward heaven. 

This was God's desire. To transcend the 4,000 years of history means that Jesus had to take control of the Israelite nation. However, Jesus could not do that. Why could He not do so? 

If you were to ask today's Christians what should be chosen before selecting the Israelite nation, they would say it is the apostles or Judas Iscariot. But it is not them. Jesus had to choose the family of Joseph before selecting the Israelite nation. 

Originally, when God sent Jesus, He sent Him based on a tribal foundation. That is, because He was established as a descendant of David, Joseph had to absolutely obey Jesus for the sake of the descendants of David. Jesus stood in a victorious position based on this tribal foundation and had the mission to establish the nation before God, but that tribal foundation was completely destroyed. Moreover, even John the Baptist, who was Jesus' cousin, acted on his own accord and ultimately forsook Jesus. Because of the failures of the family of Joseph, the foundation of the tribe of David, which had been prepared for 4,000 years, disappeared. That tribe stood in a position completely unrelated to Jesus. 

So, out of necessity, Jesus had to establish Peter, the fisherman, in place of the tribal foundation. You must understand the pitiful feelings of Jesus, who had to establish even a fisherman in this way. How can we just praise Jesus Christ, the Son of God, without knowing this situation? 

Jesus came as the Son of God to save all people, but because He could not resolve the heavenly procedures necessary to stand boldly before all people, He was overwhelmed by them. Ultimately, He found Himself in a position where He had to bear the cross and prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane. 

"My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will." (Matthew 26:39) 

However, Jesus had to complete His position as the Messiah. 

Jesus came to this earth as the representative of all humanity to redeem all people. However, it was not that there were no conditions for Satan to accuse Jesus. Because of this, Jesus had to go through such heavenly procedures again. How serious and pitiful must Jesus' heart have been in such a position? 

Throughout the 4,000 years of Israel's history, the effort God made and the efforts made by the generations of the Israelite people were great, but we must understand the unjust reality that Jesus, who came as the protagonist to establish the new Israel and build a new heaven and new earth, had to fall on the path of the cross instead of making a new start. 

The tribe that stands before heaven, that is, the tribe of David, is in the position of Abel, while the Israelite nation is in the position of Cain. Therefore, from a providential perspective, the Cain-like Israelite nation must completely unite with the Abel-like tribe of David centered on Jesus, thereby establishing a victorious foundation of expectation for the nation before Jesus. 

If the faction of the tribe of David, representing the nation, had become one with Jesus, they would have achieved the expectation of substance centered on Jesus. Without this expectation of substance being fulfilled, the expectation for the Messiah cannot be formed. This is how the principle works. 

However, because the priests, scribes, and the entire Jewish community rebelled against Jesus, the Cain-like Israelite form fundamentally broke apart. Thus, entering into the realm of Satan, Satan directly attacked the tribe in the position of Abel. 

In this way, Jesus, who lost the tribal foundation, found Himself in a fate where He could not escape the persecution of the nation, being pushed around and ultimately advancing to the cross. Therefore, Jesus desperately clung to His twelve disciples, trying to find a way to avoid this, and even prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane. However, because He could not trust all twelve disciples, He chose only three whom He could trust until the end and took them to the Garden of Gethsemane to pray the final prayer of negotiation, whether heaven would break or the earth would break. Yet, even during that critical time, the disciples were asleep. They were asleep. 

The disciples did not know the position in which Jesus was suffering. How much must Jesus have longed for someone who could be in a position to unite with Him? 

Jesus stood alone before God, in a position where He could unite with God, while the disciples were in a position where they could unite with Satan. This is the tragedy of the human world. Who is Jesus? Jesus is the true father of humanity. Today, false parents have arisen on this earth, and those false parents have become enemies of God, so all of this must be reclaimed. Being born again means being born a second time. It means that because they were born wrong, they must be born again. This tremendous, sad, and tragic fact remains in our life path that must be resurrected. 

Jesus came to this earth as the Savior of all people, and at the same time, as the father of all people. God is a God of love. What will God use to save fallen humanity? If God sends a Savior as a servant, then He is a God who treats us humans only as servants. In that case, we humans can only believe in God to the extent of the responsibilities of a servant. Even if He sends a Savior to us in the position of a brother, that cannot be God's complete love. So what is a position higher than that of a brother? It is the position of a father who seeks to find a son on this earth. Therefore, Jesus came to this earth in the name of the Savior, but the content was that He came to find true children with the relationship of humanity's true father. 

Yet, the children killed their father. It is already a sorrowful matter that Cain killed Abel in the history up to now, but they even committed the sin of killing their father. Therefore, countless people today, no matter how good they may be, cannot escape the judgment of the heavenly law. 

Regardless of Satan, all fallen tribes must bear the providential responsibility and come to save humanity. The Messiah, who came to establish us as His true sons and daughters and take us to the complete heaven, was welcomed but was instead killed. 

Those who have that blood relationship are the humans on this earth. The mission of the Lord of the Second Advent 
For this reason, Christianity cannot help but be a religion of tears. You must understand this clearly. Yet, despite this, they say that if you just believe, you will go to heaven. If they had been unfaithful and disobedient before God from the position of adopted children, they would fall under the conditions for accusation, but if they had completely united centered on Jesus, it would be the same as standing in the position of being grafted onto Jesus. Thus, after winning in the satanic world, they can love their children even more than they loved the people of the satanic world. Only then can God's love finally settle in.

When one sees God's love, one can understand that the heart that loves the children of the satanic side is different from the heart that loves the sons and daughters restored to the original world. Therefore, the teacher is the same. Until now, it has been an era of loving those without external relationships, so to conclude the responsibilities of that realm, one had to occupy a position that could align with that realm. This is the will of heaven. Because the teacher was in such a position, he could not love his parents and family even once. He received a heavenly gift that possesses the priceless value that cannot be exchanged for anything in heaven and earth, but he could not kneel before his parents and say, "This is what this word means and that is what that word means." Moreover, his elder brother knew that his younger brother was the best in the spiritual world and the best in the physical world, and he devoted himself to the teacher. This could be known even through prayer. Yet, he could not tell that elder brother what mission and responsibility he bore. Compared to Jesus, who was disbelieved by his own parents and siblings, one could say that the teacher has triumphed. Furthermore, the teacher's parents loved him very much. His mother loved him dearly in her family. However, the teacher never conveyed the principle words to his maternal relatives.

Because the teacher could not stand in the position of Mary and Jesus, he could not indemnify that. Therefore, he could not say anything to his parents and siblings. He also heard all sorts of criticisms from his relatives, but he could not express his convictions to them either. Thus, even with relatives, the teacher devoted all his sincerity and efforts to pioneering the foundation of restoration for the one person who is the only one on this earth, focusing on distant strangers. This was aligned with the 1960s. Only after overcoming such a hill does one become qualified to love parents, children, and relatives.

In the growth process of restoration, the problem lies in the growth stage. In the three stages of restoration—rebirth, growth, and perfection—growth is always the issue. If you draw a straight line through rebirth, growth, and perfection, growth is positioned in the center, and this is always indemnified centered on this. While it is a straight line when drawn as a line, the existence world is three-dimensional, so it refers to the central position. Why is the second number always an issue in the Bible? It is because the second is positioned at the central line of the heavenly law of rebirth, growth, and perfection; if you occupy this center, you occupy the whole. That is why God always fights with Satan centered on the center.

In the Adam family, the providence continued centered on the second son Abel among the three sons Cain, Abel, and Seth, and in the Noah family, the providence continued centered on Ham among Shem, Ham, and Japheth. Looking at the Abraham family, due to the mistake of the three offerings of the first generation Abraham, the process of fighting Satan while offering the only son Isaac took place. Moreover, when we look at God's sons, the first son is Adam, the second son is Jesus, and the third son is the returning Lord. Among them, the fight was centered on the second son, Jesus. Thus, the providence has always been carried out centered on the second son. Isn't that so?

Then, what fell when viewed from the family? The rebirth-level Adam family fell, so it must be restored through the eight members of Noah's family. Therefore, the primary standard by which God can fight with Satan is the Noah family. The second starting point for restoration and the starting point for judgment are all centered on the Abraham family. This is the three generations of Adam, Noah, and Abraham, that is, the three stages of rebirth, growth, and perfection, and it is three generations in seeking the ancestor of faith. Because Adam could not become the ancestor of faith, Noah was established, and because Noah also fell due to the mistake of his second son Ham, it continued until Abraham became the ancestor of faith. Isn't that right?

The 36 families are the ancestors replacing the lost 36 generations. The fight between Cain and Abel in the Adam family, the fight between Shem and Ham in the Noah family, and the fight between Esau and Jacob in the Abraham family have extended to this day. So what must the history of restoration do? Because the history from Adam to Noah and Abraham failed, it must be found again. The vertical history of humanity is 36 generations. These 36 generations are the ancestors of humanity. To set these 36 generations horizontally, those who have come to this earth bearing the responsibility of parents must indemnify all historical matters. Then, what is the central issue in restoration? Initially, it was centered on Noah, so the three sons of Noah are the issue. The condition of having restored the Adam family is established. The history of 6,000 years thus far has been for the purpose of establishing this family, so when the three sons of Noah are determined, it will rise historically, and they must stand as ancestors. If it is established that they are the ancestors and that a victory realm is prepared where they do not receive accusations from Satan, then even the descendants of Noah can enter a realm where they do not receive accusations from Satan. From this perspective, the fall has been a matter of the past, present, and future, with the present centered on the past being cut off and the future being severed. By receiving blessings and being connected to this land, the married families who lived their lives according to their own desires and have passed into the spirit world are becoming one with the earth. At this time, all ancestors in the spirit world can return to the earth. Do you understand? So, how happy would the spirits be? That’s why when they communicate, they dance and celebrate.

<Words> You have likely heard many times that after the first 7-year course ends, we must embark on the second 7-year course.  
At this moment, we are starting the second 7-year course, which is significantly different from the first 7-year course that was a bloody struggle to fulfill the long-awaited hope. This difference is due to the historical context and the distinct mission we must undertake.  
Regret regarding the first 7-year course  
We, who are gathered here, are already people who understand the mission. We are those who have resolved to dedicate our lives for the purpose and have walked the path of struggle. Therefore, you must become more aware that you have made a vow before God to take on this historical mission in this year, connected by God's blood and flesh. Additionally, we must renew our resolve in light of the past.  
We know that God's intention was to conclude the 6,000 years of sinful history during this 7-year course. We also recognize that since Jesus 2,000 years ago, Christianity has labored to conclude the providential connections that remained, building the altar of bloody martyrdom.  
We are aware that there have been countless prophets and ancestors who came to this earth for the purpose, leaving behind a sense of regret while only stepping into the satanic world with their hearts, swearing to establish the purpose and going to the place of sacrifice or death. They have all hoped for this 7-year great tribulation to be the final decisive period.  
Thus, the demands of history have focused on a specific era and point, presenting a decisive battle between Satan and God. So, who is the one responsible for concluding this battle? It is not the many people living on this earth. It is not even the entire 30 million people of the Korean nation. Neither the world nor the 30 million people of this Republic of Korea know who they are.  
The world does not know that the group pursuing unification, which has been oppressed and chased among this nation, bears this significant responsibility. However, God knows, and that is why He has been pioneering the difficult path with us until now.  
When we think of this fact, it is a privilege that only we possess, a pride that only we can have. We are well aware that this 7-year course has been a meaningful period in which we could feel this in the historical process.  
Because of this 7-year course, the teacher has emphasized that each of you must fulfill your duty of loyalty and filial piety before God whenever there is time. We did not promise to establish the duty of loyalty and filial piety in a glorious victory or luxurious position. We vowed to walk the 7-year course at the place where blood, tears, and death intersect, on the final path that no one desires. We resolved that if tears come, we would shed even more tragic tears, and if we faced death, we would bear the historical regret that no one else could carry. Reflecting on that path, there were many tearful stories.  
We have walked a path that others cannot possibly understand. However, when we consider that the sorrow we have faced is far less than the sorrow of God, who has worked hard to lead us and pioneer the internal and external paths, we must once again feel how shameful and sinful our position is for not having fulfilled our responsibilities in the past. However, this does not mean that the entire nation has been led before God because of the sorrow we caused Him, nor does it mean that this world has entered the heavenly realm.  
Therefore, at this point, we must once again adjust our collars and make a full advance with this nation.  
We must once again establish the second 7-year course before the world. When we think of this, you are in a position where you must once again invite God and restart the path of labor. You must recognize that this is an unjust and frustrating fact.  
The 6,000 years of labor have been a tedious path, but we must feel ashamed that the labor of God, who has worked hard on the turning point of this 7-year course of indemnity, has been greater. Furthermore, we must solemnly repent for the fact that we could not conclude the providence with the first 7-year course and are now walking the second 7-year course with a national regret.  
In this new year, I ask that you resolve in your hearts to reorganize the responsibilities you have not fulfilled and to offer meaningful offerings before the Father in the newly starting second 7-year course.  
The significance of the first 7-year course  
You know that the last first 7-year course was to prepare for the conclusion of the teacher's 21-year course. Although you participated as individuals in the last 7-year course, from a historical perspective, you represented countless historical figures. The sincerity you invested during that period will not be in vain. It will remain as a connection on earth for eternity and will become a foundation where many good spirits can offer their praises in the heavenly realm. Such a period will not come again on this earth. When we think that the time has concluded with the year 1967, which just passed a few moments ago, you must dedicate all your intellect for the purpose.  
Knowing the regret that history carries is a matter of great sorrow, but it is something we cannot change, having become a story of the past. To resolve the regret of that history, we, who have raised the banner of unification on the Korean Peninsula, have come out while enduring persecution and arrows of criticism. However, we did not stop on the path we were walking. Even when we were oppressed and chased, we did not neglect to grow internally while also organizing externally. Because of this, now, there will be no one to block the path of the Unification Church anywhere on the Korean Peninsula. The determination to establish a standard that cannot be blocked by any swords or guns has brought about this tremendous victory from a heavenly perspective. Because we established these conditions, we were able to create a new history centered on them.  
We are grateful for these facts and have borne the difficult path of the past with meaning, but now we must organize the entire nation for the remaining internal areas. It is your mission to organize this nation and to embark toward a new world, and we must all remember that there is a mission for the teacher to ensure that you fulfill this mission.  
So, what path should we take this year? This is a task that cannot be overlooked, especially at the beginning of the new year, for the Unification Church members spread across the nation and the world. This year, let us take a full offensive leading to peace, that is, let us focus on the slogan of a full advance and start the second 7-year course.  
In the first year of the last first 7-year course, the slogan was to make it the year with the greatest achievements of our lives. In the second year, it was to become God's representative, in the third year, to become one who can show and boast, and in the fourth year, to become a victorious subject.  
When we think back on these slogans, what do they mean? What does it mean to make it the year with the greatest achievements of our lives? Because humans live in the satanic world, it means standing in a position where we can distinguish ourselves before the satanic world, having the conditions for indemnity, and restoring all historical sins to achieve victory, that is, to return to the individual. This is the hope of humanity. By returning to the individual, we become children of God, having the authority to judge Satan on behalf of God.  
Then what follows? It is to become one who can show and boast. This means to practically demonstrate the appearance of being a child of God on this earth. It means to show this personally, domestically, nationally, and internationally. Then, it was to establish a victorious subjectivity from the individual level to the national level. That was the purpose of the 7 years.  
Preparation for a full advance  
This year, we must engage in activities under the slogan of a full advance. The issue at this time is how to ensure that every member of the Unification Church participates actively day and night without exception. How can we make sure they are active without rest? First, we must solidify our internal organization. When you are active, there must be a goal. To achieve that, you must organize all internal matters so that you can achieve that goal on your own. Since you are people engaged in church activities, to make a full advance, the entire Unification Church must quickly expedite internal organization across all areas.  
To organize internally as individuals, you must become someone who can be recognized before God regarding the word of God, centered on your faith. You must also be someone who can be recognized before God in reality, and you must possess the active power to take responsibility for the lives of others and generate new life from there.  
Therefore, each individual must organize internally to act centered on the purpose. You must have a standard that can be deemed right in the sight of God. To do this, you must study the Principle. Of course, if you are a member of the Unification Church who has walked the normal path during the last 7-year course, you should have passed the Principle exam.  
You must not be someone who follows the word unconditionally. First, you must become a being with subjectivity through the word, that is, you must have the character that can create as the subject of the word.  
However, when we look at those who have studied the Principle in the Unification Church until now, many are people who cannot find emotional or personal standards and only work and move with the word. If you do not become someone who can speak with that inherent subjectivity, the people connected by that word will have no relation to you. So, how do we complete our character? We must receive God's approval. To receive God's approval, we must confront Satan and achieve victory.  
Then, after acquiring a substantial character through the word, what remains? It is to subdue Satan. So, where will we subdue Satan? It is not in the house where we live or in the workplace where we operate. We must confront Satan in the place where the highest authority of a nation resides and subdue him. Moreover, we must subdue not the Satan who accuses individuals but the Satan who accuses on a national level. Only then can we become children of God.

Because of this providential content, the Unification Church has faced national opposition until now. We cannot possess the value of a victorious character nationally without enduring persecution in the church, family, society, and nation. That is why God has allowed many trials on our path.  
From this perspective, mere truth is not enough. Therefore, when we speak, we must do so in unity with the truth. We must not be led by the word but must dominate the word. Thus, even Satan must acknowledge God's word as true. To do this, we must have the empirical conditions to subdue Satan with the word.  
Organize internally  
So, how do we acquire empirical conditions? Since the invasion of Satan began with the violation of God's heart, the primary standard to judge and subdue Satan is to revive God's heart. In other words, you must understand that the foundation for victory is established by reawakening God's heart. That is why, in the end, there is judgment of the word, judgment of character, and judgment of heart.  
The word, character, and heart are the standards of judgment, but what level should that standard be? It must be above the standard before Adam and Eve fell. If not, we cannot appear with the banner of victory from the position of having found the word again. We cannot stand in the position of having realized the word and its substance, nor can we stand as someone called by God before the substance of the word, who has inherited God's heart. That standard must be determined at a level higher than that of Adam and Eve before their fall.  
That is why the Unification Church teaches the heart of God in the era of completion. Adam and Eve could not comprehend God's heart when they fell at the completion level of growth, but we in the Unification Church have been teaching God's heart in the era of completion. We have been teaching what God's will centered on completion is.  
Therefore, unless we stand at a position above that standard, we cannot settle the standard by which Satan caused the fall of Adam and Eve, so you must go to such a position.  
However, when we look at the world’s humanity, there has not been a single person who has gone to such a position until now. We must go to that position. That is why the word of the Unification Church is a privileged word. The practice through the word of the Unification Church is a privileged practice. From this perspective, each of you must complete your internal organization. The question is whether this is in place. That is why, to engage in continuous activities, we need internal organization that can support this.  
Establish a sense of purpose  
Next, your sense of purpose must be clear. No matter how complete your internal organization is, you must not wander aimlessly without a goal. You must set a clear goal and understand what the path toward that goal is and what the value of achieving that goal will be.
You must clearly understand what it is like.  
Now, since 1968, members of the Unification Church are in a situation where they must make a full advance. They must march forward centered on a distinct goal.

After solidifying internal adjustments, you must work sincerely and diligently.  
We must not forget the path that Jesus took from the Garden of Gethsemane to Golgotha.  
"Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; yet not what I want, but what you want." (Matthew 26:39) Just like Jesus prayed, you must have a heart that does not doubt even a little, saying, "Not my will, but your will be done." The strategies and methods of the Unification Church are different. Our strategy is to shed tears, blood, and sweat, to be beaten and trampled upon while taking back what was lost. As a result of this strategy, we have avoided the sorrowful position of the defeated. Since you have already experienced this and brought about the results of victory, you must continue to develop this strategy without rest. We must become people with a meticulous sense of purpose in the position to replace Jesus, who resolved to step over death.  
Feel the sorrow of the defeated in advance.  
You must understand that on the day we fail, that is, on the day we do not achieve our goals, we cannot avoid the sorrow of the defeated. Rather than breaking midway while heading toward the purpose of fulfilling God's command, let us imagine what it would be like to be a defeated person in advance. Let us feel the sorrow of the defeated in advance.  
Even Jesus felt the sorrow of the defeated at the last moment of his three-year public ministry, in the Garden of Gethsemane, while offering his final prayer of lament. Therefore, we should not feel it only after being defeated, but rather feel it before reaching that point.  
What would that sorrow be like when defeated? Let us predict the position of the defeated. First, when you stand in the sorrowful position of the defeated, the enemies will rejoice. The first seven-year course, like the great tribulation.

Now, I will briefly discuss the nature of the first seven-year course and the second seven-year course that will begin this year. The seven-year course is a period of historical indemnity. Jesus had to overcome the global indemnity course centered on the age of 40 from the age of 40. The Bible states that he had a three-year public ministry, but originally, it began at the age of 27. The seven years from 27 to 33 years old constitute the first seven-year course, while from 34 to 40 years old constitutes the second seven-year course. Therefore, that person must suffer on this earth.
