<Words> Today, this time, I will speak briefly on the title of "The Limit of Restoration."

At first, among all people, there may be some who do not understand what the term "the limit of restoration" means. Restoration means returning to the original state. The limit refers to the highest standard required for restoration.

Why is restoration necessary? 
Everyone living on this earth is unanimously saying that this world is an evil world. We are experiencing the harsh reality that our wishes cannot be fulfilled and that the opposite reality is dominating society, and we are well aware that we are struggling to escape from that environment.

How did such results, such circumstances and content come about? It is because the original good center could not start from a normal standard and instead began from an abnormal standard, that is, from a starting point opposed to goodness. Therefore, we have become individuals who must struggle to break through this world and return to a normal world, that is, the world of creation that our hearts desire, and we can assert that this is the reality.

However, in the real world, we cannot find God's love, God's ideals, or a united world centered on God anywhere. When we see that the world of true ideals has not been realized on this earth, we cannot deny that we are in a position where we must clear away the world of evil.

Today, Christianity speaks of the end times. It says that the time must come when this earth will be cleansed. Because this is a sinful world, it is a time when we must establish a just and absolute standard, which you cannot help but recognize.

So why is restoration necessary? It is because humanity has fallen. Because of the fall, we must return.

Then how should restoration be achieved? It must be through indemnity restoration. Without indemnity, restoration cannot occur. God and Satan are fighting over the offering, and the path of indemnity is the way to go.

To achieve indemnity restoration, offerings are essential.

The Purpose of Jesus' Coming
Until today, there has not been a single person who can govern their body with a clear standard of conscience when faced with any problem on this earth. We know well that there has not been a single person who can govern all human emotions in accordance with the heavenly principles or the heavenly law.

That is why Jesus said that the kingdom of heaven is within your heart. He said to love me (Jesus) first to enter the kingdom of heaven. He also said to take up the cross and follow him, and to give up everything you have. Furthermore, he said that those who want to live will die, and those who want to die will live; those who want to possess will lose, and those who want to lose will possess; those who want to be exalted will be humbled, and those who want to be humbled will be exalted. Why did Jesus speak such paradoxical words? This is the question.

You possess both heart and body. However, the heart cannot be in the place of the heart, the body cannot be in the place of the body, and the spirit cannot be in the place of the spirit, which is a lamentable situation.

Our ancestors have made continuous efforts to establish the standard of the heart on this earth to conquer the body. However, despite the long passage of 6,000 years, there has not been a victor who has completely conquered the body centered on the heart of all humanity.

Then, who will take responsibility for solving this lamentable problem? Since we have not found a firm center where the heart can govern the body with a deep emotional connection to the heavenly law, how can we conquer such human hearts before the one who possesses the heart of the heavenly principles? This is an important issue. God sent Jesus to this earth to solve that problem.

Jesus came with such a mission, saying, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride." Then, what should be the standard of conscience that the bride must have? It is not the conventional standard of conscience soaked in earthly life. It is not the standard of conscience that is either angry with or proves the morality of this world.

Also, what is the true image of the bride? It is not the very existence of those living on this earth.

Then, what kind of figure was Jesus, who came out as the bridegroom of humanity? He was a person who cherished the heart of God and had the directionality to establish eternal standards of conscience and the body by experiencing that heart. If he had not been so, Jesus could not stand in the position of the true bridegroom of humanity.

Therefore, if God exists, what kind of world does God aim for? It is not this cultural and civilized world of today. This is the world that our ancestors should have left for future generations.

The Place Jesus Went

In the course of history, God has been conquering individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world. So what is that conquest? If it cannot be done with words, it must be done with force. Therefore, there cannot be a history without war.

We know that this era is the end time of 6,000 years of history. God is looking for a victor who has the authority to conquer the whole from oneself, placing everything before God and aligning it with His will.

Our ancestors in the past ventured to conquer their own selves and went forward without caring about any difficult paths or the paths of pioneers. However, humanity living in the 20th century today is living in an environment different from that of the ancestors. That era was a providential age concerning individuals, families, nations, and states, but today is an era of providence concerning the cosmos, so if we have any adventure, we must have the spirit that no one can venture more than I in place of 6,000 years of history.

Therefore, in such times, those who cry while holding onto themselves will not be able to build a heavenly family; those who cry while holding onto their families will not be able to build a heavenly society; those who cry while holding onto their society will not be able to build a heavenly nation; those who cry while holding onto their nation will not be able to build a heavenly world; and those who cry while holding onto the world will not be able to build the cosmos.

Thus, you must have the conviction that you can draw your personal feelings up to the world, explain all historical content, and assert that you have established a global reality. You must engage in a life-and-death struggle to determine whether you live or die.

Noah struck his own body to find the standard of the family. For 120 years, he struck his body, enduring all kinds of ridicule and scorn, and even when faced with unjust circumstances, Noah held onto the heart that God had established, saying, "Will that heart change?" and centered around that standard, he struck his body for 120 years.

If Noah's family had overcome all worldly desires and conditions while longing for the nation, God would have fulfilled His will through that Noah's family centered on the nation. However, Noah's family could not overcome all the twists and turns in the process of their labor. If Noah's descendants had held onto the heart of the standard that Noah established and looked toward the nation, God's will would have been fulfilled through that nation. But because Noah's family could not establish the familial will, God's will, which was to be fulfilled through that nation, was shattered.

Still, God's providence to fulfill His will continues. It is the time of heavenly order that does not allow one to hold onto a broken individual. Just because a family is broken does not mean that heavenly order does not move. Even if individuals are shattered, heavenly order moves forward. Even if individuals are broken, it is the time to establish families, so God is working on the providence to restore individuals and families. Also, just because a family is broken does not mean that providence can be delayed there; therefore, God moves forward to restore society. In this way, God is expanding the environment while timing the providential moments.

If you know that God is alive
God, who lost Noah as an individual and his family, worked through Abraham 400 years later. However, since Abraham also lost the will, God worked through Moses 400 years later, and just as He had to match the environmental conditions when He established Abraham, He established the law of circumcision to include even the Gentiles.

He pushed them in while looking forward to a time when they could do so. The timing of pushing them in coincided with the national providential period, which is why God established Moses as the vanguard of adventure on behalf of the nation.

He appeared as an explorer with a new resolution in the process of spying out the unknown land of Canaan. The path he took to oppose the palace and lead the Israelite nation was not a smooth one. It was an unknown journey. No matter what difficulties lay ahead of him, he did not care. How could his heart change when seeking the promised land that God had promised to his ancestors? Even though he lived in Pharaoh's land, his heart was filled with the conviction that he should sing of happiness in the land of Canaan.

Thus, Moses's mission was to instill an indomitable spirit in everyone and to pioneer the path of advancement. However, although Moses started with 600,000 people, he lost them all during the 40 years in the wilderness. <Prayer (I)> Father! On this holy day, we bow before Your presence with our inadequate selves, so please accept us.

Father, whether in a place of joy or a place of sorrow, we earnestly hope and wish that You will lead us to the homeland where we can experience Your love.
Father, we know well that our inadequate selves cannot absolutely reach the standard You desire and seek. We want to become a passive entity, not an active one, to support You with a humble heart, so please allow us.
Help us to realize that we cannot approach You with anything of our own. May all that comes from us disappear, and may we be governed entirely by Your omnipotent power, allowing us to advance to the position of being embraced in Your love and created anew. We earnestly wish and hope for this, Father.

272   The homeland

We believe there are Your beloved children scattered here and there who long for this place in their hearts, so may Your love be with them as well.
Father! Even if we have nothing on this earth, may we have one heart that can align with Your heart, and through that heart, may families, clans, and nations align with Your heart and completely establish a unified world on this earth. We earnestly wish and hope for this, Father.
From the first hour to the last hour, we earnestly ask that You allow us to dedicate this time entirely under Your direct guidance. <Words>
I will speak for a moment under the title of "The Country of Our Hometown." The country of our hometown is, in other words, the country that must be restored.

Humanity has longed for the world of our hometown. The world we live in now is not a happy country where all human hopes are fulfilled. It goes without saying that individuals live in such a world, families do, and nations and the world do as well.

But could the world that humanity has longed for be such a world? Or would it be a higher and more precious country of hope? And is there any ideal country that our original mind desires?

We acknowledge the fact that humans cannot be born by themselves. Such humans have built history until now and are still doing so. Because of this, humans cannot achieve the country that the original mind desires with their own abilities.

Therefore, we are hoping for that country that the original mind desires. We are hoping that it will come quickly rather than having the mindset of "I will create it." We know very well that this is the heart of people spread across the world. In other words, it is not from a subjective standpoint that we say we will firmly create such a country, but rather we are hoping that such a country will come quickly.

When we see that humans are not in a subjective position but rather in a relative position, we can understand that for the country of our hometown, or the ideal country, to be realized on this earth, there must be not only the power of humans but also some absolute power behind it.

This is because this world is the fallen world spoken of in Christianity. Because this world is a fallen world, it is a world of sorrow, a world of pain, and a world of lamentation. Therefore, Christianity says that this world must be judged and that we must go to the hometown that our original mind desires, that is, to a new ideal world.

Not only Christianity but also many religions scattered across this planet have established central thoughts that admire such an ideal country. Therefore, we must surely find the country of our hometown and become the people of our hometown. You must understand that this is the wish of all humanity.

Many people live in this world today, but they are not the people of our hometown, and many nations exist, but they are not the nations of our hometown either. Looking at the current era, which is moving towards an ideal world, we can see that the present world is not the world of our hometown.

The more we acknowledge the fact that today's world stands in such a position, the more we must question whether we should welcome this entire environment or reject it. If the current nations and world do not possess the conditions of our hometown that can satisfy us, what should we do about it? Should we just leave it as it is, welcome it, or reject it? We cannot deny that we are faced with this dilemma.

However, high-level religions have denied compromising with the present world and have taught that it should not be permitted to place purpose in the present world. In other words, they have completely denied everything that is lived according to one's own will centered on the individual.

When we see this, we cannot deny that even if there have been wonderful worlds throughout history, those worlds were also like that, and even if a more wonderful and higher world is established in the future, that world cannot be accepted by those who long for the country of our hometown.

So how should we deal with this? We are in a position where we cannot welcome it or punish it, and you cannot deny that we humans living on this earth are in such a situation. Therefore, it is a fact that everyone is in the realm of the Fall and is in a place of sorrow, pain, and lamentation that cannot be added to.

That sorrow and pain lead to death and destruction, and ultimately, we cannot avoid facing the end. Thus, throughout the ages, something has warned through the hearts of people that the end of this world is approaching. If there is an absolute being, that absolute being must desire individuals, families, nations, and worlds that can resonate with the will of the absolute being. Therefore, we must understand that the absolute being could not help but announce that the end will come to this earth.

For this reason, it is acknowledged by all that the end of the world will come. The fate of humanity is such that such words arise.

Why must this world be settled? People living on this earth today have a desire to live for thousands of years. They always wish that their lives will be the source of happiness and that they will reach happiness. However, no matter how much they pursue happiness on this earth, because they were born in an unhappy position, they cannot find happiness anywhere.

Ultimately, it is a life that must meet the end of unhappiness after going through an unhappy environment. Because humans do not have a place to establish the hometown family, hometown society, hometown nation, and hometown world that the original mind longs for, you must clearly understand that all that those humans yearn for, desire, and wish for cannot be achieved based on the current living environment.

Therefore, we must find a way to deal with this. It must be cast away. How wonderful it would be if there were a way to cleanly resolve this all at once on a global scale! We must find a way to deal with this. Whether one is a good person or a bad person, everyone on this earth must break through and deal with this. If there are those who love and care for this world, they must research ways to handle this. And to deal with this, we must engage in some social or global activities.

However, no matter how much humans try to deal with this, if they do not know an absolute standard, it cannot be a complete resolution.

In other words, even if the current humans handle things well in their own way, it does not become a standard that can fulfill the expectations of personality, family, and society that can transition to the world of our hometown. Humans alone cannot do it.

You cannot control your own heart. To be autonomous, you must become the self that claims "this is mine." And to have that autonomy, you must be able to govern and judge yourself. Yet, despite this, how is it that you cannot control your own heart?

History flows without finding a fundamental solution. If I had started with myself as the motive, I would automatically be able to govern the results of that. However, my birth was not motivated by my own heart. Among those who are destined to die after 10, 50, or even 90 years, there is no one who has the authority to govern their own heart and hold up the banner of victory.

From this, we can understand that our hearts did not start from the place of birth. Our original mind did not start from a foundation where I could initiate, govern, and act as I please; it flowed down from something unrelated to me. In other words, something motivated it to flow down. I am in the position of an object, not a subject. It is undeniable that there was some source of life that could influence me, which is why my being could flow down from there.

Since we are living in an environment where I cannot do as I please, even if we devise some method to deal with the world, we must understand that if that is not completely aligned with the standard of the original mind, the issues that have been dealt with will again encounter the connections of denial. 

In light of this, even if the current humans devise a method to deny or punish something in this world, it cannot become a foundation that can eternally align with our hearts or guarantee a new world. Therefore, we must understand that a new ideal world cannot be established solely by human power.

Who in this world wishes to perish, and who wishes to be unhappy? Yet, looking at the mainstream of history until now, countless people have suffered misfortune and perished, regardless of their intentions. This shows that there is something caused by a fate that humans themselves cannot control.

In this path of fate, which cannot be removed or defended against, humanity is groaning. In other words, although humans search for direction amidst suffering, they are in a position where that direction is vague, akin to groping in the dark. It is like trying to break through the void in a fog.

Therefore, even though I say, "This is what I want," and devote all my life energy to it, it often leads me down the opposite path. Many people throughout history have harbored great intentions and worried about the future of the world and humanity, yet they have not found a fundamental solution, and history continues to flow.

In the past, many people struggled to find ideals, but Jesus also lamented, "I came to cast fire upon the earth, and how I wish it were already kindled!" (Luke 12:49) and "I have much to say to you, but you cannot bear it now." (John 16:12-13). From this, we can see that there was something deeper within than the external manifestations that appear in real life. This is the motivation and origin that can judge social evils and the wicked world, and you must deeply contemplate this fact in your hearts. You must understand this clearly. Is that not so?

The conditions for unhappiness must be removed by oneself. And you must recognize that all the harsh environments are surrounding you. Those of you in the Unification Church, who are in such an environment, must have the heart to break through.

Then what is required here? No matter how much humans try to establish the country of peace, they cannot achieve a global peace with anything in the human world. If it were possible, many sages of the past would have already established that world with their sincere efforts.

Today, people are struggling to explore ideals based on existentialism and realism within the developed scientific civilization. However, unlike this era, the sages of the past entered deep mountains and valleys, asking, "What is the heart? Where is the hometown of the heart? What is it that the heart seeks to establish?" They devoted all their efforts to internal content. Thus, they sought to establish a standard of personality that could create a world of goodness, a heavenly kingdom on earth that could bring joy to humanity. Many people prayed and devoted themselves to finding this.

However, when we see that they could not find the standard to organize the earth and resolve this world, can the Lord come and save the world? Can you achieve the ideal world, the utopia that our lives long for, the country of our hometown?

The problem is that your hearts and bodies are not united and are divided. Therefore, if the external body and the internal heart become one, there will be no problem. Thus, when we ask whether the heart and body are unified, the body is the enemy. The heart wishes to go straight, but the body wishes to go in the opposite direction.

When you say that someone's heart is twisted, have you seen the heart being twisted? How does that person's heart know what it knows? It knows through their actions. A straight heart is also known through actions. A person with a straight heart acts in a unified manner because the body moves as the heart wishes.

To become a straight line, two points must connect with each other. In other words, the heart and body must be united. A straight line must pass through one point and another point. One alone is not enough. A twisted heart means that one point on that straight line is misaligned. Therefore, the heart and body must absolutely become one. In other words, the ideal personality that can support each other must be a unified heart centered on the ideal, the center of ideals, and the conscience of ideals.

What will bloom from that unified position? In a place where the heart and body are one, the love that God wants to dwell in forever will blossom. Jesus had a heart that loved others to the extent of sacrificing himself centered on love. Every religion has a heart that is willing to sacrifice itself centered on love. You must have such a heart not just for a moment but eternally.

Just as the solar system revolves endlessly according to certain principles, our hearts must also revolve in unity. Then, can there be a person who can achieve a higher level of unity that aligns with the power of natural law? There must be someone somewhere.

When we look at the structure of humans, we unknowingly fall into the mystery of the scriptures.
Modern science may boast of its advancements, yet it has not fully elucidated even a single aspect of the human eye. There remain fields that require research spanning thousands or even tens of thousands of years.

Therefore, if a person emerges in this world who has reconciled their body and mind into one unchanging heart and body, what do you think that person would be like? What kind of love would dwell within them, and what would their understanding of ethics and morality be? Furthermore, what kind of views on family, society, nation, world, and the universe would be formed from the love that erupts from their heart? Think about it for a moment.

Religion places significance not on achieving its goals in a relative world but on exploring its own essence. For this reason, it seeks to escape the world in search of the original world, the world of the heart. Thus, religion does not start from a place that seeks recognition in this world but from a position that absolutely denies it.

A religion that has a clear logical basis for denial can become a global religion, placing heaven and earth on the boundary of denial. Therefore, to be a religion that saves the Republic of Korea, it must either uplift or bring it down. Isn't that right?

If a person has found their original home and achieved a unified personality of body and mind, that personality is not one governed by the rights of personality established in the real world but is a standard of personality that can transcend and govern all of reality. Thus, those who cannot establish such standards cannot build their original families, tribes, or nations.

The standard of the original mind and the original home

One must feel ashamed and acknowledge that life is something they cannot control. Therefore, whether one is talented or not, if the heart and body do not harmonize, that household will decline and become miserable. In other words, individuals who have not unified their hearts and bodies have formed families, making harmony difficult. Thus, no matter how enjoyable or peaceful life may seem, such families will ultimately fail. This is why the heart and body must be completely unified around the original standard.

Does a person's standard of heart break every time they go in and out of prison? Even if it happens dozens of times, the standard of heart does not break. It may not function, but it does not break. However, I have seen many people struggling to overcome the internal hardships that accumulate in proportion to the number of crimes committed.

The damage caused by the battle between my body and mind is greater than any suffering from the world's tribulations or the damage from wars. You must understand that there is a mountain of sorrow resulting from the defeat of the heart.

People often lose to their bodies in this battle several times a day, yet they remain unaware of it. However, they remember vividly when they tripped over a stone and broke their leg years ago. In other words, many forget the defeats of their hearts due to the battles with their bodies.

When considering this, even if you shout loudly, it is merely a display of a defeated soldier holding a sign. However, originally, the heart should triumph over the body, always governing it. Yet, because this has not happened, the heart and body have pursued different directions.

When we refer to someone as a person of character, we do not mean their appearance, educational background, career, or status. We look at how principled they live. Therefore, it is not about emphasizing external splendor or diversity. A person of character is someone whose heart serves heaven unwaveringly and can live according to God's will.

The teachings of ancient sages emphasized revering heaven centered around the heart and loving all humanity. They taught to love heaven, love the earth, and love humanity.

So, does your heart possess the elements to connect with heaven one hundred percent? Does it have the elements to connect with all humanity one hundred percent? Does it have the elements to love the earth one hundred percent? Do you possess these?

When analyzing the original heart itself, there exists a natural heart capable of loving heaven, the earth, and humanity. This original heart arises automatically, no matter how much one tries to eliminate it. It is because of this original heart that humanity has historically pursued the ideal world, the land of the original home. Thus, the action of the original heart begins with me.

When someone becomes a certain way, people only see their facade. However, to truly know that person, one must look at their heart.

Materialism cannot create a world of happiness.

What kind of world have we been living in until now? It is not a world for the satisfaction of the heart but rather for the satisfaction of the body. However, one cannot achieve happiness of the heart with what the body desires. In other words, one cannot create their happiness centered around an external world focused on the body. That is absolutely impossible. In other words, it cannot be achieved with money, power, or anything else.

Yet, if one possesses something external and says, "Hey, body, isn't this enough? Can't you be happy with this?" will the heart respond, "Yes, you are right!"? That is when it becomes most difficult. Therefore, when the body seeks comfort, the heart commands, "If you do that, you will perish. You must do it this way."

For this reason, even if one claims to dominate the world with external things, they will ultimately fail. If you have money, do not claim it as your own but rather as part of the world, as belonging to heaven and earth. You must do good deeds, and the heart commands this. This cannot be denied. You must understand this.

What kind of world are we living in now? It should be centered around the heart, yet it has become a materialistic world where people do not even consider whether they have a heart. This can be seen in the reality of education, which is entirely focused on material civilization. This precious and noble heart is neglected for the sake of visible money. Furthermore, it has reached a point where people deny the existence of the heart and even deny the existence of God.

The ideal couple refers to a couple formed in a position where Satan cannot invade. In other words, it is the establishment of a marital relationship based on God's justice, having indemnified and restored the vertical history horizontally. Therefore, the ideal must be centered on God. 

If it is not the ideal expectation before the fall of Adam and Eve, a new ideology cannot start. You have not stood in a position where you have fought to reach a place where Satan cannot invade; rather, you have stood in a position that believes in and follows this ideology. Therefore, if you do not establish emotional expectations and substantial expectations, blessings will return to nothing. 

Love is eternal. Therefore, love must remain in the eternal way. 

In love, there is no revolution, no development, and no regression. 

The fall is the establishment of an illicit love centered on Satan, so it must be restored to a love centered on God. 

After achieving individual completion and relational completion, one must receive recognition through love centered on God for the true ideal to be realized. 

Unification can only be possible when true men and true women stand in a position recognized by God. That is the wedding feast of the Lamb. 

New love centered on God, that is, love based on the laws of creation, is where God's ideal finally begins. 

Love is what can completely govern the whole. To govern with one-sidedness is not love. 

When God's will can dwell in a body where Satan cannot invade, and when individuals who have completed their personalities can stand in a family where Satan cannot invade, and when nations and states that Satan cannot invade unfold, then heaven will be realized. 

Good must be established in a place where it has been persecuted to be fully established. Only in such a place can Satan naturally surrender. 

Heaven must be established through families. Jesus could not go to heaven because he did not establish a family. 

Good does not escape from evil; it fights and breaks through evil. This is why there is much grace where there is much sin. When the time comes, religions that deny reality will perish. 

Ideal love is realized in families. However, God has not had true sons and daughters. He has not had true siblings, nor has he had a spouse, nor has he been able to become a true parent. Therefore, it is God's will to achieve these things. Only in such places can love dwell. 

In places where such love is realized, people abandon everything in the world to come. 

Today, the most important thing is love. Judging the love centered on Satan is the great judgment. 

Teaching the heart of Adam and Eve before the fall is the Unification Principle. 

Jesus came as God's perfect son, but he could not establish the standards of marriage and parenthood.
The original human being must be able to feel the four great hearts of parents, grandparents, siblings, and children in relation to others. That is why a family is necessary. *

36 Families' Responsibility
<Summary of the Words> We must understand that the 36 families represent the three families of Adam, Noah, and Jacob. Sacrificing individuals to establish conditions for indemnity is for the purpose of establishing families. Although Jesus spiritually triumphed, He could not establish the realm of Israel on earth, which is why He is returning to establish the realm of Israel in the spiritual world on earth. The returning Lord also begins to establish the earthly realm of Israel from individuals. We must connect the spiritual First and Second Israel to establish the Third Israel on earth. To do this, the returning Lord must find and establish the First Family (the family of Adam), which represents the First Israel, the Second Family (the family of Noah), which represents the Second Israel, and the Third Family (the family of Jacob), which represents the Third Israel. Therefore, the 36 families must become the ancestors of humanity. Because Jesus could not fulfill His responsibilities as a parent, the returning Lord must resolve this and take on the second responsibility of indemnifying the mistakes of Adam and Eve. To take on such responsibilities, the 36 families must uphold the will of the returning Lord (the Second Ancestor) and follow His path to form the Third Israel. In the future, they must organize a global tribe. They have the responsibility to unite those who have married at their own discretion and those who have formed families. Therefore, they must become one with the Teacher. Because there is a root, they must realize that they exist as branches.
