Parents are the starting point of history
Today is the ninth Parents' Day. When viewed from the perspective of the family, there will be days to celebrate the day the parents of that family got married, and there will also be days to celebrate the birthdays of children born. Additionally, there will be days to celebrate when those children grow up and get married. From a national perspective, when a nation gains independence from oppression by another country, that day may be designated as a national holiday. There are many days of celebration like this.

However, when viewed from a providential perspective, all such days have nothing to do with God. No matter how much the people of the world stay up all night praising and celebrating such days, those days are created in the fallen human world and are not necessary for God to establish His restoration providence and will. Therefore, such days must inevitably pass away.

We must understand that the people who lived through a historical era or those living in the present have unforgettable days that they celebrate and love in their own ways. However, when viewed through the lens of God's providential will, the days that people celebrate in a worldly manner have no connection to God. Therefore, such days will inevitably disappear from this earth.

We must recognize that when those who lived through history go to the spirit world, the days they celebrated will become conditions of sorrow based on the standards they celebrated. Today, there may be people who boast of having a day to celebrate that can be proudly shared with the world. However, they must understand that when the day comes to celebrate with God at the center, the day they celebrated will become nothing more than a shameful condition.

So, what is the day that people most commonly wish to celebrate? Without a doubt, it is the day of birth. What comes next? It is the day of the wedding. And what follows? Perhaps the day of passing? The day of birth is the most important day, followed by the day of receiving a partner, and then the day of giving birth to children.

No matter how many days there are to celebrate in the world, any day that deviates from this principle can be a relative relationship but cannot occupy a direct position of heart. What do these three important days signify? The first hope of fallen humanity is the completion of individuality, which is rebirth centered on a resurrected individual because the individual has fallen. The second hope is the completion of relationships, meaning that the born individual receives blessings. The third is the reproduction of good children.

So, who is an unhappy person? It is not someone who is unhappy because they could not attend a local celebration, nor is it because they do not have a national holiday or a global celebration. No matter how good a day may be, it cannot compare to a day that is directly good for oneself. The directly good days are the day of one's birth, the day of determining one's partner, and the day when new children are born between husband and wife. Therefore, a person who does not have such days is an unhappy person.

If this is true for people, what about God? God is the same. Then, does God also have a day of birth, a day of marriage, and a day of giving birth to children? This question arises. 

The day God is happiest is the day Adam was born. This day is the first day of God's start as the God of the substantial world. In other words, the first substantial start from which God can be born as a cosmic value begins with Adam. If there were no Adam, there would be no value of God. There may be inherent value, but there is no relative value. In other words, the actual value of something is determined by the relative position in fulfilling desires regarding a certain purpose. Therefore, the day God is happiest, in other words, the day He created all things, is the day He established Adam in this universe. Next is the day Adam gets married. Why would God be happy about Adam's wedding? Because Adam's wedding, from a heavenly perspective, is God's wedding. Then, what about the day of giving birth to children? Likewise, Adam's children become God's children. Here, the center for constructing the flat heaven, the substantial heaven, is established. The children of Adam are the first start in constructing the flat heaven and the substantial heaven.

The day God is happiest is the day Adam was born, so we must celebrate this day. But who has ever celebrated the day Adam was born? Has God ever proclaimed, "O humans, the day my son Adam was born is such and such a date!"? No. Adam was born, but we do not know on which day he was born.

The next day that God might like is the day Adam holds a feast. But did Adam hold a feast? He did hold a feast, but it was a feast that the enemy stole. So God could not have a joyful day. God lost everything and could not have a joyful day in this bright universe. Ultimately, God has not had a joyful day.

What can God be happy about if He has not had a joyful day? Ordinary Christians who do not understand this think that the glorious God sits on a high throne, commanding the world to move at His command, but this is a misunderstanding. Given this situation, would God be happy or sad? That God is infinitely sad. He is the God who must resolve His sadness. Who would like a God who cannot resolve His sadness? Moreover, if this is the case in the world, no one would want it. However, if it is their own child, they may want to like it even if they do not, and if it is not their child, they may not want to like it. Today, such a world is unfolding.

No one has started from the day that God can be happy about. That is why today humanity is bound by the statement that they are the descendants of the fallen Adam and Eve. What joyful day can there be for those who were born without a joyful day? No matter how much people dream and sing of happiness, it is entirely a path of sorrowful life. Ultimately, they fall into a place of self-pity.

In such a place, it is absolutely impossible to have a substantial world of heaven, that is, a world of heart that can stimulate joy in connection with heaven and earth. Therefore, this world must pass away. Such days must be discarded. So, in the religious world, one must deny oneself, one's family, one's nation, and the world. Must we live while longing for that world and just long for it from that place?

To find heaven, one must turn back and seek the path of restoration. Then, will one not be able to welcome the day that God will be happy about? Will the people of Israel just be sleeping on the day that God will be happy about?

Awake, O all people! Speak, O all people! Dance, O all people! If there are sons and daughters of God and His people, can He just smile and be happy alone while establishing them? When it is a good time, everyone must rejoice together. Even the flying chicks must match the rhythm to be good. If such a day comes to the beautiful land of Korea, will it only be a day for Korea to rejoice? Everyone would wish for a heaven where they could come and go thousands of times a day on this earth. We hope for such a day to come to this earth, but we have not yet had such a day. No matter how much we long for it and want it, if that day does not appear, we cannot have it or see it. Therefore, humanity hopes for the day of freedom and the nation where equality, peace, and happiness can be sung.

We hope that that day and that nation will appear.

The Reality of History and the Content of Providence
The history of humanity should have been a continuous joy celebrating the day of birth, and that joy should have been accompanied by love. Parents have a layer of love that cannot help but love their children. When that child grows up, there is also the desire for them to grow up quickly, as if wishing for the child to grow up in a day and serve their parents from the next day.

However, in the world, there are people who are the only sons of five generations, and moreover, a woman who marries into a family that has raised such a son with a single mother, no matter how good and excellent her character is, does not receive affection. Instead, she is often disliked by her mother-in-law. The love for her beloved son is added to the love between husband and wife, but why does jealousy and envy follow? This is the heart of Satan. God wants to see mutual love. Today, those who understand our ideals should rejoice and praise the love between sons and daughters-in-law. If the daughter-in-law loves her son, she should dance with joy, so why is there jealousy and envy?

The joy of the day a son is born contains love for the son, but within that love is also love for the daughter-in-law. When the two love and care for each other, from God's perspective, would He say, "Hey, move aside! You are obstructing traffic!"? Even on a highway, no matter how much traffic is obstructed, He would say, "It's okay!" and would not push through.

God created Adam and Eve after great effort. He created the universe to create them. Thus, after creating Adam and Eve with great difficulty, God must have been indescribably happy. However, there must be a time when He could be even happier, which is the time when His created sons and daughters become one, that is, when Adam receives his bride. This joy connects to all things born in heaven and earth, and it connects the center of love to all humanity. From there, tribes will emerge, and if they explode in harmony, this world cannot help but be drawn in. Then, you will all be born resembling God, and those who do not resemble God will strive to resemble Him.

So, have you been born resembling God, or are you trying to resemble Him? Which is it? You must at least try to resemble Him. If you were born resembling God, what day should you rejoice in? If God resembles you, it is one thing, but if you resemble God, what day should you rejoice in? You should rejoice in the day you were born. Next, you should rejoice in the day you got married. And you should rejoice in the day you gave birth to children. This is the origin of history, and the reality of history and the content of providence have developed to achieve this.

Jesus and His Bride
God has been working hard to find such days until now. God first sought to establish a son and then a daughter. So, who has the salvation providence centered on until now? It has been centered on men. Looking at history, we can see that men fought for the providence. If there is a top person in a fight, there is a family that excels in that fight.
There must be such a race and nation. God must have a first-class nation. The idea of a chosen people emerged in the historical process to create such a foundation. The one responsible for guiding the chosen people with that idea is none other than man. 

When God created the heavens and the earth, He did so relatively. Man is internal in this flat, horizontal world. Therefore, unless a man can stand internally and rejoice, anything achieved in the external world is all meaningless. Thus, a man seeks to establish a standard by which he can rejoice in the internal environment. And that standard of joy is not personal; it is a standard by which he can rejoice centered on a nation. This is what we aim to create. In this way, Israel was to create a chosen nation larger than the scale of the chosen people. In other words, it was to find a man who could rejoice centered on the nation.

Then, whose joy is it that rejoices in that nation? It becomes God's joy. 

Looking at the historical process up to now, it has been a providence of salvation centered on man. Is that not so? In that historical process, through the path of historical suffering filled with sorrow, pain, and misery, a central figure who loves heaven and loves the earth has emerged, and he is the Messiah whom all people awaited. 

Through the birth of the Messiah, that is, Jesus, God was able to feel the joy of the time when the son, who was lost in the Garden of Eden, was born again. Then, what must that son do after being born? It is not about fighting well or earning money well. He must get married. But did Jesus get married? No, He did not. Why could He not get married? Because although Jesus was well-prepared as a bridegroom, there was no woman who was prepared as a bride. 

What was Jesus' desire? It was to establish the day of resurrection that could resolve the sorrow of restoration before the world. The day of His birth became a day of joy, but the question was how the day of God's glory would come. 

God's wish was to welcome a day of blessing centered on Him, but that wished-for day collided with a cliff. In other words, the ship that was running toward its purpose encountered a whirlwind, breaking its mast and losing both direction and purpose. 

Why did Jesus need a bride? God needed a woman who could have relative content before the men who worked hard to prepare the foundation of Israel. Jesus came not for His own sake but through history. He fought from Abel through Noah, Abraham, and so on, spanning thousands of years. There was no woman with a historical heart before such a man with a historical heart. 

If such a woman had appeared and could stand as a relative existence before Jesus, He could have simultaneously indemnified all the historical sorrow of His time. Then, it would have been a new start with Eve alongside an unfallen Adam. Therefore, such a being like Eve must come forth and indemnify all historical matters in that time and make a new start. Otherwise, the foundation of restoration and indemnity cannot be established. 

The lonely Jesus 
Although man came through thousands of years—because the found bride of Adam ruined the great work of heaven in a single day—women must also clear the entire satanic world in the restoration. Therefore, Jesus must connect all historical indemnity conditions to Eve. Eve must indemnify them throughout her life. In a position where she did not understand the will, she must come to know the will through Jesus and hand it over in that time. This means that Eve, who originally fell by listening to Satan's words in a position of knowing nothing, returned by listening to the words of her original husband. It is said that there was no woman who could inherit this historical connection and take responsibility for the position of Jesus' bride at that time. 

Think about it. Jesus came to resolve the historical sorrow of 4,000 years and to raise the flag of liberation before all people. How serious must each moment have been for such a Jesus? He must have moved with the heart to move and shift heaven and earth all at once. Yet, where was Israel, which could correspond to that? Where did the so-called learned lawgivers and priests go? They were busy opposing Him, making a fuss about their own greatness, and drove Jesus away. Thus, instead of lowering the anchor of hope on this land, they had to lower the anchor of despair. 

When faced with such a fate, how serious must Jesus have been when He went to the Garden of Gethsemane? 

"Father!" The prayer He called out was filled with the heart, blood, sweat, and tears that could pierce through 4,000 years of history. Blood, sweat, and tears are not shed in vain. Jesus prayed with blood, sweat, and tears to save the fallen Israel. Yet, Peter, John, and James, who did not understand this heart of Jesus, were sleeping. How heartbreaking was that? 

Before such a heart of Jesus, there was no one with the conviction to deny themselves and step forward, capable of overcoming mountains. It was a shocking era. Still, Jesus endured. However, I believe that at that time, Jesus taught incorrectly. He had too much love. He was always on the side of His disciples. Even when the Pharisees criticized them for rubbing grain in the fields, He defended His disciples. 

However, such a Jesus was not recognized by the public of Israel or the Jewish community. He was not recognized by the lawgivers, scribes, or patriarchs. Moreover, He was even rejected in His own family, the household of Joseph, born of David's lineage. Rejected by His family and betrayed by His disciples, Jesus had nowhere to go but to the cross. As He was dying, He said, "Do not weep for me, but weep for the sons and daughters of Israel." He asked them to weep for the coming day of liberation for Israel. 

Yet, there was no one who could love Jesus, shed tears for Him, and convey His circumstances again after crossing the hill of the cross. Thus, even now, 2,000 years later, Christianity has become what it is today. If one fails to fulfill their given responsibilities and missions, they will perish. Jesus left the standard of the family for future generations as a promise. How shocking it is to think that we will meet again after going away! 

The path of Jesus and the path of the Teacher 
The path of Jesus is a path that cannot be made even in 2,000 years. How long did they wait to meet that Lord, and how many ancestors melted their bones in miserable tears while dying on that path? It is astonishing. This nation and people thought that the Lord would come here or there, and no matter how much they waited, the promised Lord has not come. Only the waves of death, that is, the waves of familial death, tribal, national, and global death, sweep through this era. Unless we face an era where we can advance, the Lord cannot come before this nation. This is what this nation did not know. 

However, this nation must pass through the first, second, and third stages centered on the Teacher to reach a global era. Therefore, families and nations must be ideologically restored and establish a new national system. How can we establish this nation as a leading nation in the world without receiving help from America or any other country, suppressing communism, and making it an ideal homeland? The Teacher has always kept this in mind. However, as the spirit of this nation has become blurred, the traditions, culture, and ethics have also become blurred… Everything is being swept away by the waves of death. 

So, should we not raise questions here, delve into them correctly, study, and understand? Is the problem how we live now? We only knew the direction and speed of the ship we were on, but we did not know that the wind was pushing us. If we are not careful, everything will be shipwrecked. We do not know that we must understand the speed of the wind and turn the helm to change direction. 

On the path of faith, we must go straight toward the goal. In the global end times, storms will come crashing in. Therefore, even if one has the right purpose at that time, if they cannot set the direction, they will be swept away by the storm. Those who do not know the winds and currents will be shipwrecked. 

Until now, the Teacher has taught about the love problem of the family, such as the relationship between parents and children or the relationship between husband and wife, establishing a standard for the family. This has not been touched by anyone throughout 6,000 years of history. Nowadays, all relationships in families, such as parent-child and husband-wife relationships, are breaking down. This is because Satan is trying to break this. This signifies the end times. When such a chaotic era spreads globally, shining from the east and west, it means that the Lord has come to this earth and has established Himself. 

What is the desire of Jesus, what is the desire of God? The day when God is most pleased is the day Adam was born, and the next is the day He receives a bride. That is why Jesus said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the brides." In the past, Christians thought that men were also brides. However, men are servants and archangels. They are like the archangel who violated Eve. Therefore, when a man establishes the external, the internal is done by a woman. 

To reach the level of completion 
The history of grace began with grandmothers. People over 80 years old, like Anna, were the center of the history of grace. The history of grace in the past was centered around grandmothers who were 70 or 80 years old. Then it came down to 70s, 60s, and 50s, and when it reaches the 30s, it signifies that the Lord's time has come. 

Then what must He do when He comes to this earth? He must get married. At that time, will God look upon it with tears or with laughter? Just wait and see. In the course of human history, there is still hope that must go beyond the standard of completion. Adam had to connect this standard of hope and cross into the realm of completion. However, because Adam could not cross it, the Lord who comes must take on that responsibility. Thus, the Lord who comes is taking on the responsibility of Adam and coming to this earthly world. 

However, even if someone is in the growth stage, no matter how much they communicate spiritually, they cannot ascend to the level of completion. To ascend without fulfilling all the necessary conditions is like invading the position of parents. Therefore, to ascend to the level of completion, one must meet all internal and external conditions. That is, they must represent heaven above, represent the earth below, integrate all historical processes behind, and stand confidently in the present, uniting all humanity for the coming era. Only such a qualified person can cross this line, having received recognition that they have come with authority greater than that of the old Adam. Before that, one cannot cross this line. Thus, Jesus came to this earth and started from the foundation of victory established by Jacob's family, Jacob's tribe, and Jacob's nation, centered on Israel, which had triumphed over the satanic world. 

To receive atonement, we must have a heart that can unite with the one central person who can offer a sacrifice for all people. Then, all those who are united through that one person will receive indemnity. Do you understand what this means? Thus, the bridegroom comes centered on Israel, which is one of the world’s nations. 

When it comes to the standard of the fall of Adam and Eve, they become adopted children. Adopted children cannot inherit simply by remaining still. They must establish conditions that show they were loved more than the biological children by their adoptive parents. Only then can those adoptive parents joyfully grant them inheritance. This must be clearly understood. 

Israel is a nation of adopted children. Therefore, all that nation must have a heart that loves God and is loyal to God more than Adam and Eve did before their fall. Without that greater heart, they cannot be restored. They must rise to that standard. That is why John the Baptist, representing Israel, came out into the wilderness for over 30 years, eating locusts and wild honey, to establish the condition of loving God more than the ancient prophets. However, his position was that of a wild olive tree. 

The Israelites who have received the price of sin 
Then, who must go out to the realm of completion at such a stage? According to the principle of creation, humanity and parents must go out. Adam and Eve are the parents of humanity. The parents of humanity must come to this earth and fix what was broken due to the fall. Initially, Adam was drawn into the fall centered on Eve. According to the principle of creation, Eve was created through Adam in the Garden of Eden. Therefore, it is not about bringing Eve from the satanic world; it is about reclaiming Eve, who was taken by Satan. She must be reclaimed and recreated. Jesus came to this earth to do this. But who knew such circumstances? 

What did Jesus do for three years after coming to this earth? What are the 12 apostles? The Teacher considers them trivial if they only bow down to Him. In Christianity, they talk about Paul and how great he was, but what is so great about Paul? When the Teacher points out their mistakes, they are flustered. Today, the theological trend has turned Christianity, which was to be Jesus' religion, into Paul's religion. 

If Jesus had come, He should have indemnified and restored everything. He should have indemnified and restored everything lost in Eden. Furthermore, Jesus had to choose and establish one woman on this earth. If Jesus had started anew from a family that everyone could praise, what would have happened? It could have been a bright new morning where all things could joyfully welcome Jesus. However, that did not happen, and noon has passed, leading into the sunset, and instead of receiving praise from the crowds, He was forced into the lonely path of death, surrounded by Satan, fighting against death. This is a shocking situation. The nation of Israel has made mistakes. The nation of Israel finds it difficult to be forgiven for its mistakes, even after 4,000 years, 6,000 years, or countless millions of years. The heavenly world is eternal, and no one can erase the sins committed by that nation with blood. No matter how earnestly a tribe tries to erase it, there is no one within that tribe who can erase it. 

Because the nation of Israel committed sins that cannot be washed away in providence, it became a nation that is scattered and wandering in the world. They were slaughtered as a result of the sin of killing Jesus, suffering, being enslaved, and disappearing as sacrifices, with six million being massacred. The fact that Israel has now gained independence shows that the time has come for the Lord to come to this earth. 

Since the second Israel does not have the foundation required by this land, it must form a spiritual foundation to connect the actual second and third Israel.
It is in the chapter. With the return of such an era, the nation that could not fulfill the mission of the First Israel was able to revive as Israel gained independence in 1947. 

Thus, until now, Israel has been cornered by enemy nations. From a spiritual standpoint, being surrounded by the Arab world, which was once the archangel, is akin to the situation where Jesus was driven away and killed in the past. If they sincerely believe in God with a single-minded determination to find the Israelite realm and repent for the wrongs committed in the past, God will lead them into an era where they can embark toward a new heaven and earth. The miraculous victory achieved within a week in the recent battle with the Arab world was also helped by God. Moving forward, they must dedicate themselves with the intention of protecting the holy land of Jerusalem. They must also possess a heart that exceeds the standards of the fight, and if they do not have the deep heart of repentance that Jesus had in wanting to establish Israel, the nation of Israel will face a counterattack. Looking at them recently, they seemed to rejoice and dance after winning, but I felt that they lost the emotional standard to welcome God after the dance.

The Korean people also danced with joy after the liberation on August 15, but the teacher looked on and prayed with tears in the room. Yesterday's joy should not turn into today's sorrow. This must be deeply ingrained in the bones and passed down as a traditional thought, as the patriotism of this nation.

The Unfulfilled Will of Jesus
Who can be the support for this? Who can bring God into the national reality and establish a national standard that can please God? There is no one. 

Until the completion of the growth stage, it is the standard that Adam and Eve ascended to in the past. That standard that Adam and Eve reached still remains. Since Adam and Eve fell after reaching that point, it is a standard left by historically failed parents. From there, the world of Satan was formed, and Jesus paved the way for Israel centered on the heavenly national standard regarding this world of Satan. If the Israelite nation at that time had welcomed Jesus in accordance with His will, they could have ascended to the standard of completion from Jesus' perspective. This standard is the seven-year course. 3×7 is 21, and the 21-year course is an extension of Jacob's 14-year course, centered on the Jacob family, which was the standard for restoring Canaan. Therefore, it must be fulfilled within these seven years. It is a shocking fact.

Jesus had to fulfill the internal standard of will before starting His public ministry at the age of 30, but He could not. Of course, it was not because Jesus made a mistake, but during the seven-year period from age 27 to 33, He had to establish the internal standard. From age 27, He was to establish a national standard centered on the seven-year course, and then create a new second seven-year course to establish a global standard, so that in the spiritual course, the nation of Israel could surpass the heavenly standard as a world nation. The seven-year course from age 34 to 40 would lead to the great tribulation of seven years. Thus, the 40-year peak is a problem. The teacher is also currently crossing the 40-year peak. After crossing Jacob's 14-year peak, the standard of family blessing is finally determined. Only then can there be blessings for all things. It cannot be done haphazardly. If the nation of Israel had ascended to this peak on a national standard, they would have entered Canaan's welfare.

What was the world of the archangel that Adam faced during the time of Adam? Satan is lower than the archangel. Therefore, the world of Satan is not a problem. Until now, we have sought national and ethnic standards to determine the parental standard, so in the end, we will be able to govern the world nation. Do you understand?

The Foundation of Happiness
Jesus came as the Son of God. Since a son was born, God could celebrate a joyful day. This is restoration. Since He came as a son, He must get married. After determining the counterpart for the son and establishing the day of the son, the day of the parents must be established. One must become a parent to have a son, right? If one cannot give birth to children, one cannot become a parent. They can be a couple, but they can never be parents. Only after giving birth to sons and daughters can one understand the love of heaven and earth, and only by understanding that can one know the way of humanity. One must understand that.

So, it cannot be just children, nor can it be just couples. One must reach the position of parents. In other words, one must reach a position where they can establish the love of children, the love of couples, and the love of parents. Therefore, the happiest day in a person's life is the day when such things can be found.

There is no day happier than this. If such a day is not established, the expectation of the son-in-law centered on God will not be fulfilled. Restoring the son-in-law expectation centered on God, children, couples, and parents is the foundation of happiness in life. 

Even in the world of Satan today, people living alone are not considered happy. In their hearts, there is always the autumn wind blowing. So, which is better, the autumn wind or the spring breeze? The autumn wind is indeed cool and feels good, but internally, it carries a pressure that seems to hasten death, while the spring breeze is warm but can be cold when you dig deeper. However, it is in that place that the harmony of heaven and earth unfolds. Therefore, a person living alone is like someone living in an autumn garden, while a couple living together is like someone living in a spring garden.

In the spring garden, bees and butterflies fly, but how many bees and butterflies fly in the autumn garden? Of course, there are butterflies in the autumn garden, but think about it. Bees and butterflies are meant to fly in the spring garden, not in the autumn garden. However, in autumn, there is a lot of busyness. All the grains must be harvested, and preparations for winter must be made against the cold. But spring is the time to loosen up. Even while walking down the road, if there is a grassy field with mirages rising, one would want to take a nap there. Do you prefer spring or autumn? I prefer spring.

So, no matter how much happiness is sung about and how things are said to be, is living alone happiness? When a couple lives together and one person dies, they cry out in sorrow. Can one prepare their own path alone? Why do we say it is pitiful to be without a partner? It is because they are disqualified in front of all the important days that heaven and earth can rejoice in. They are out of alignment with the laws of heaven and earth. Clearly, only through that law can the fortune of heaven and earth turn, and the conditions and motivations for happiness be determined. 

Feeling sad is also because one is far from that law, and in terms of that sadness, the law of heaven and earth does not comply. What does it mean to feel joyful and good? It means that there is a place in the world that welcomes that person. Sadness is a place of being cast out. Joy and sadness are thus divided.

From the Wild Olive Tree to the True Olive Tree
The more one approaches God and surrounds Him, the happier one becomes, because that is the principle. Therefore, the spiritual world is an ideal world centered on God, moving according to the rhythm and wave of God's love. Thus, if one does not cultivate elements that can harmonize with that world on earth, there will be no harmony there. To do this, one must perfect the love of children, the love of couples, and the love of parents.

So how should humanity be restored? First, one must ascend to the world of adopted children and then ascend to the world of sons. Then, by welcoming that son and aligning with the ideal counterpart, one must lead them to the position of parents. This is the history of restoration. Analyzing history is simple. Yet, here, they are fighting and making a fuss about what is what among themselves.

For Israel to transition from the adopted children to the direct lineage, they must receive grafting. To receive grafting to transition to the direct lineage, the love relationship and emotional relationship that Adam and Eve had with God were not deep enough, leading to their fall, so that love must be better than that of Adam and Eve. Without establishing a standard of being better, they cannot follow at all. Therefore, they must receive grafting from Jesus. Grafting does not mean taking Jesus' arms or legs and attaching them. It means learning the laws of how Jesus loved God, how humanity should live, how to honor God, and how to love neighbors from Jesus, and considering that as one's own life results in receiving grafting from Jesus. In other words, the wild olive tree transforms into the true olive tree. This is where the kingdom of heaven on earth begins. Through this kingdom of heaven on earth, one can enter the kingdom of heaven in the spiritual realm. Especially women must understand this clearly.

Unification Church members aim to enter the kingdom of heaven on earth. So, what door must one pass through to enter the kingdom of heaven on earth? To enter the kingdom of heaven on earth, there must be parents. Originally, one should be loyal from the position of a child in heaven, but having been born while fleeing and being chased, they were born in a state of refuge. One leg is broken, and the head is twisted... It is a situation where they are treated and barely kept alive, carrying them around. It is not pleasant, is it? It feels bad, doesn’t it? Think about it. You have nothing to boast about.

The Day of Parents and the Teacher
In the spiritual realm, the period corresponding to the realm of paradise is the seven-year period. This means that during this seven-year period, the members of the Unification Church worked according to the standards of the 7,000 years of history that the spiritual realm has been longing for. Do you understand? Then, who should those in the realm of paradise follow? They must follow the True Parents. Therefore, if our Unification Church has something better than general churches, it is that the standard for calling the Father and Mother is different. Those in paradise cannot call like that. However, you have come to represent the earth, the Mother, who is the Holy Spirit, has come, and the Parents, who represent heaven, have come with their names, so it is an immense honor. Do you understand?

Until now, no matter how well one believed in Jesus, they could not become a fig tree that bears fruit. When Jesus entered Jerusalem from Bethany, He was hungry and looked for fruit on a fig tree but found none, so He cursed it, and it withered, right? That fruit is the Lord of the Second Advent.

What our Unification Church has contributed before heaven and earth is the establishment of the Day of Parents. This Day of Parents was truly hard to find. For the Day of Parents to emerge, one must go through the process of being adopted and then the process of being a child to reach the standard of God's counterpart. If this is not established, the Day of Parents can never emerge.

Jesus had to lift the nation of Israel to this standard while on this earth. This period is the seven-year period from age 34 to 40. However, Jesus could not walk this path. The teacher also took seven years praying centered on the Republic of Korea. If the established church had accepted the teacher, he would have already become a global teacher. Then you would have discovered a great teacher. However, you have not yet discovered a great teacher. You do not see the name of the Unification Church teacher spreading worldwide like wings. Thus, you have become a failure. It is a shocking matter. You have given birth to children, but they are all disabled children, with crooked arms and legs. Yet, you cannot just leave them behind. After giving birth to such children, it is not that someone made a mistake in giving birth to them. It is not that the father made a mistake in giving birth to such children. The seeds were good, but the field was bad. Therefore, it is not that the Republic of Korea is bad. In a few generations, it can improve according to the laws of genetics.

On a Day of Parents like today, even if the teacher speaks to prominent people from various countries, it would not be enough, but to speak with you is shocking. Would you feel good? Would God be pleased?

What would have happened if Jesus had established the will of the national standard? If He had stood in the position of fulfilling His responsibilities as a son starting from the position of parents, He would have had to determine the counterpart. Then, automatically, sons and daughters would emerge. Likewise, our Unification Church is doing such work. We must fulfill the mission of the son that Jesus could not complete. In other words, we must determine the relative standard that Jesus should have fulfilled and work to restore the adopted children to direct lineage. That is why we are doing this. Until now, centered on the 60s, we have blessed 36 families, and based on those families, we have blessed 72 families and 124 families. This work is to liberate all spirits and the spiritual realm throughout history.

The Background of the Establishment of the Day of Parents
When establishing the Day of Parents, a standard that exceeds seven years was necessary. If it were established carelessly, it could not be in accordance with the original meaning of the Day of Parents. Thus, it would inevitably be subject to Satan's invasion. Before that, one must fight against the world of Satan, experiencing both bitter and sweet, to establish a Day of Parents that has true value. Therefore, after surpassing the seven-year peak, the Day of Parents was established along with a new Day of God. Establishing the Day of God centered on this year is a miracle among miracles in history, and there is nothing happier than that.

Originally, the day when the love of God, centered on Adam and Eve, is fulfilled is the Day of God, the Day of Parents, the Day of Children, and the Day of All Things. However, in the Unification Church, the Day of Children was established, leading to the establishment of the Day of Parents, and the Day of Children and the Day of All Things were established, pulling out the seven-year peak. Although Israel expelled Jesus and forced Him onto the path of the cross, today, after going through the history of the seven-year course, if we unify the world centered on the Republic of Korea on that standard, the expectation of providence will rise, and it will never go down.

We have already created such a historical environment, and moreover, because Jesus, who represented the global standard, has set a standard before God, the Day of God has been established according to the historical environment that can welcome God. Thus, the lost Day of God, the Day of Parents, the Day of Children, and the Day of All Things, these four major holidays have finally been determined centered on the altar of the Unification Church. You must understand that this fact is the greatest victory achieved in the providence of restoration through the historical process.

Therefore, those who could not follow the seven-year course leading up to the Day of Parents cannot become children. They are either those who felt dissatisfaction and fell away or those who were expelled from here. That is why the teacher said to follow him no matter what happened during the seven-year course. Until 1967, he said, "Let us shed tears together, feel loneliness together, and suffer persecution together."

You who follow the teacher's path cannot be without loneliness. You have been pushed and chased, leaving traces of tears. The reason we have walked this path is that without doing so, we could not cross the seven-year peak. Before crossing this peak, one cannot enter heaven. The teacher has worked hard while walking this path centered on the Republic of Korea.

Now, the teacher is no longer needed. The Day of God has been proclaimed, so there will be divisions within both the democratic and communist worlds. Now, globally, all phenomena are corrupt and collapsing, and it is a time when we must drive out even the last one. The United States is currently embroiled in the Vietnam War. If the teacher were the president of the United States, he would have the confidence to elegantly orchestrate the world.
What we are doing is, upon closer inspection, something that cannot possibly fail. In the face of such a destiny, we have entrusted everything to God and have fought until the end. Therefore, even if we are crowded and chased, we must fulfill our responsibilities with the dignity and authority to establish God. We must establish the dignity of having fulfilled our responsibilities even in places of crowding, being chased, or imprisoned. God has set the standard of victory before Satan in order not to succumb to him. Thus, by establishing this standard, we can bring glory to God. This is our responsibility in the history of restoration.

**Parents are the Turning Point of History**

The path that the unification group must take

We have established Parents' Day, but this Parents' Day should not become a day that only the Unification Church celebrates. It should not be a day that only we can welcome. It must be a Parents' Day that all people of the world can celebrate. 

On this day, you must understand that the heart of the Teacher, who is still groaning to overcome the long-standing grievances of history, is present. Therefore, with a desperate heart, we must prepare for the day when the sound of liberation and the shouts of freedom can fill the world, breaking apart this world of sin. We must fulfill our mission as liberators. If we do not do so, we cannot say that we have fulfilled our duty as the sons and daughters of those parents.

This day is not just for a small group within the Unification Church to celebrate; it is a day for all people to celebrate. It is a day that can be praised throughout history. It is a day that future generations can commemorate and celebrate as a day of pride, joy, and glory. Who knows that such a day of celebration has occurred today in the land of Korea? Even now, many do not know what time it is or whether time is passing or coming; they are not even dreaming of it.

In today's world, where justice and injustice intersect, we must strive diligently to fulfill our responsibilities. Therefore, this year, we must reach a conclusion. Up until now, centered around the 1960s, we have been in a position of being attacked, and we have not had a time to launch a full-scale offensive. However, now is the time to resolve that long-standing grievance on a national and global scale.

We have had God's Day, Parents' Day, Children's Day, and All Things Day. We must long for this day, praise it, and resolve all grievances tied to it so that all things can welcome this day as our day.

God is longing for such a day. Therefore, it is our responsibility to once again traverse the Korean Peninsula with a full-scale advance and to gaze upon the world stage while seeking the final battle.

We must always be fervent in that mission and burn with that mission, becoming a nation that can proudly proclaim the authority of the Third Israel before the heavenly kingdom of tomorrow, and we must become such sons and daughters. Thus, we must be individuals who can offer eternal praise to God and take pride in our existence. We are participating for the glory of that day. Therefore, we must overcome and transcend today's reality to do such work. This is the path that the unification group must take.

On this day of celebration, let us reflect on the past seven years that have passed in vain, and from this day forward, let us recognize once again the responsibility to act with one heart.

We must start with the belief that we can do it. We must participate with the heart that we cannot endure if we do not do this. Only then will your celebration of this day have meaning, and God can continue to leave a heart of hope through you. That is why you must advance. The Teacher will go with you if you advance, but if you retreat, He will leave you and go elsewhere. Will you go or retreat? "We will go."

The Teacher's position is not a comfortable and happy one. 

By welcoming this day, we can stand in a position where we can possess the value of being true children, true couples, and true parents as God desires. In that position, we must be able to stand confidently before heaven and earth, or before the world of Satan, or before the Cain-like sons and daughters. Only then can we become the people of the heavenly kingdom and the sons and daughters who can have heavenly families.

The Teacher is also walking this path now. I hope each of you recognizes that you must go this way as well. 

**Parents are the Turning Point of History**
